Twelve Banks Agree to Join the Fisheries Syndicate; Working Capital is Averagely Subscribed 87

The Ministry of Industry is preparing to establish a Fisheries Syndicate, and the Ministry has drafted a twelve-article outline of measures, which has been approved by the Executive Yuan meeting. Its capital is tentatively set at one million yuan, divided into fixed and working capital. The Ministry will first allocate 200,000 yuan as fixed capital, and the participating banks will contribute 800,000 yuan as working capital. Interest rates have also been set separately. When Minister Wu Dingchang came to Shanghai to discuss the establishment of the Agricultural Development Bureau and negotiate with the banking industry, he also brought it up for discussion. Twelve banks, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Bank, China Exchange Bank, Xinhua Bank, Jincheng Bank, Continental Bank, Yanyeh Bank, and Zhongnan Bank, agreed to join and averagely subscribe to the working capital. Qian Xinzhi, Wang Zhixin, and Gui Yanfang were appointed as committee members to draft various rules and regulations. The purpose of the syndicate is to guide fishermen to organize cooperatives and provide loans to cooperatives to promote the production of China's fisheries and improve the economic situation of fishermen. The Ministry will also task the syndicate with assisting in various plans for rescuing the fisheries industry. The syndicate's office will soon be located in the Jiangxinsha fish market.

Banking Industry's Opinion on Agricultural Development Bureau; Association Submits to the Ministry; Minister Wu Will Come to Shanghai Again to Negotiate the Subscription Amount 88

In order to rescue agriculture, the Ministry of Industry is cooperating with the banking industry to prepare for the establishment of the Agricultural Development Bureau. The Shanghai Bankers' Association convened a meeting of fellow businesses the day before yesterday to discuss this, and received the approval of all participating businesses. The deadline for participation was yesterday. The participating organizations include the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Farmers Bank of China, Shanghai Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Yanyeh Bank, Continental Bank, Jincheng Bank, Kenye Bank, Guohua Bank, Guohuo Bank, Tongshang Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Jiangsu Farmers' Bank, Donglai Bank, Zhongfu Bank, Zhonghui Bank, and other banks, as well as the Four Banks Savings Association and Zhongyi Trust Company, totaling twenty-six organizations. The Association has now compiled a list of participating banks and their opinions and submitted them to the Ministry of Industry last night for review. It is heard that Minister Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industry will come to Shanghai soon to convene another meeting of various banks to negotiate the subscription amount and decide to establish the Bureau on July 1.

Sharp Decrease in Imported Foreign Rice in the First Quarter of This Year; Decrease Amounted to More Than 27 Million Yuan; Siam Ranks First in Population, Followed by Annam 89

According to news from the International Trade Bureau yesterday, the total amount of foreign rice imported nationwide in the first quarter of this year was more than 440,000 dan, valued at 1,567,786 yuan in customs gold units, equivalent to 3,551,764 yuan in national currency. Compared with the import amount of more than 30,890,000 yuan in the same period last year, there was a sharp decrease of more than 27 million dan. Siam ranked first among importing countries, accounting for more than 330,000 metric tons, valued at 1,209,110 yuan in customs gold units. Annam ranked second, and Japan ranked third. The import amount in Shanghai in the first quarter was more than 29,000 metric tons, valued at 228,391 yuan in national currency. The detailed analysis is as follows: The amount of foreign rice imported from Siam was 3,218,653 metric tons, valued at 1,209,110 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from Annam was 97,563 metric tons, valued at 326,135 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from Japan was 1,854 metric tons, valued at 16,097 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from Dalian was 1,015 metric tons, valued at 8,679 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from Singapore was 510 metric tons, valued at 1,809 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from Korea was 386 metric tons, valued at 3,764 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from Hong Kong was 350 metric tons, valued at 1,117 yuan in customs gold units; the amount imported from India was 28 metric tons, valued at 217 yuan in customs gold units; and the amount imported from other countries was 148 metric tons, valued at 927 yuan in customs gold units. The total import amount was 440,490 dan, with a total value of 1,567,786 yuan in customs gold units, equivalent to 3,551,764 yuan in national currency. The amount of foreign rice imported in the same period last year was 4,320,887 metric tons, valued at 30,894,347 yuan in national currency. Compared with the import amount in this session, there was a decrease of more than 27 million yuan.

Jiaotong University President Li Talks About His Impressions of Visiting Suzhou and Wuxi 90

President Li of Jiaotong University recently visited Suzhou and Wuxi for inspection. After returning to the school, he made various suggestions to the teachers and students of Suzhou and Wuxi. He said, "I visited the Suzhou and Wuxi area four years ago. At that time, transportation was convenient by railway, but now there are more highways. This is a clear demonstration of the progress of China's construction, which directly and indirectly increases benefits to society. I traveled by car and saw and heard more in the countryside and cities. I felt that the climate and geography of Jiangsu are truly capable of development. Why worry about poverty and weakness? It is a pity that with sufficient food and clothing, etiquette and righteousness are not promoted, and loyalty, courage, diligence, and hard work are diminished. In the so-called scholars, farmers, artisans, and merchants, I found weaknesses of laziness, disunity, and apathy, which is truly regrettable. Those who are even slightly well-fed mostly do not engage in production, but spend their time in teahouses in the morning and evening, or play mahjong at home. There are few producers and many consumers. Who is to blame? Even in prosperous areas, there is still the problem of difficult livelihoods. In terms of growth, the countryside and the city do not cooperate in education and defense, and even among the countryside, there is no mutual assistance and promotion. In terms of occupations, scholars, farmers, artisans, and merchants each pursue their own interests, without unity. As for the progress of society and life, they seem to be unaware of or indifferent to national affairs. They do not talk about them when asked, and do not answer honestly. The national spirit is so scattered and disrespectful. In the countryside and cities, I also saw many disabled and sick people. Even among the working class, their bodies did not seem very strong, and some had sickly appearances. This is a national problem that is of great concern. I have heard that a weak country comes from a weak countryside. We must immediately remedy these shortcomings, but empty words are useless. To truly implement them, we must first know how to solve them. In my opinion, the people can be guided, but they must also be informed. Therefore, the systematic establishment of civil training classes, life improvement training classes, and economic construction training classes is an urgent task. If things depend on people, then before running these training classes, there must be adequate talent. To obtain adequate talent, it seems that the Party, government, military, and academic circles should jointly plan and proceed."

City Public Safety Bureau: Intense Work on Smoking Ban, Enthusiastic Registration of Smokers, Multiple Daily Inspections of Smoking Cases, Simultaneous Inspection of Smokers and License Renewals 92

Since the City Public Safety Bureau began accepting reports of smokers and allowing supplementary registrations in this city on the 10th of this month, the work has been extremely intense. Many smokers who had previously failed to register have been flocking to the bureau's various branches and teams to request registration for licenses and to register for smoking cessation. According to the bureau's statistics, from the 10th of this month to yesterday (the 14th), within four days, the number of people who registered for licenses totaled 851, and 135 smokers were sent for smoking cessation. Regarding the establishment of private opium dens and private smoking, the bureau has also assigned inspectors to conduct inspections in various districts. Recently, dozens of smoking cases have been investigated and handled daily. The bureau is currently conducting separate interrogations. In addition to sending those who opened opium dens to the Songhu Garrison Command for legal punishment, unregistered private smokers will be ordered to obtain licenses or sent for smoking cessation and then released, in accordance with the measures during the reporting period. Furthermore, the bureau has set the period from April 1st to May 31st of this year as the deadline for renewing the second-term licenses. With only half a month left until the deadline, and many still haven't renewed their licenses, the bureau has specially formulated measures for inspecting smokers and license renewals. It has ordered all branches to begin inspections on the 10th of this month until the end of the license renewal period on May 21st. Since the inspections began, the number of people renewing their licenses has also increased sharply compared to before.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Expresses Views on Preparations for Hide and Leather Inspection 98

It was reported in the newspapers recently that the City Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Industry, requesting a postponement of the implementation of hide and leather inspection. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, considering this matter related to inspection policy, visited Mr. Cai Wuji, Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, to inquire about the details and future measures. He was given a detailed account, which is recorded below: (The following is Director Cai's statement) The preparation for hide and leather inspection can be discussed from the standpoint of inspection policy and practical needs separately. From the standpoint of inspection policy, the Tianjin and Hankou Inspection Bureaus have long been inspecting exported hides and leathers. The Shanghai Bureau, as an inspection agency affiliated with the Ministry of Industry, should naturally implement inspection for commodities of the same nature in order to ensure the uniformity and comprehensiveness of inspection policy. As for practical needs, in today's foreign trade, only commodities of excellent quality can gain international credibility and expand trade. However, Chinese merchants often adulterate exported commodities, with many malpractices. In the case of hides and leathers, for example, second-class goods are mixed with first-class goods, goods produced in area A are falsely claimed to be from area B, and those with insufficient dimensions are stretched by soaking in water, etc. These malpractices are endless. Moreover, the adherence to traditional methods of tanning and packaging without improvement is an additional problem. If these situations are not supervised, rectified, and improved, it will be difficult to maintain a position in the international trade arena for a long time. Therefore, the need for inspection is very urgent in practice. As can be seen from the fact that well-known foreign firms and trading houses engaged in the export of hides and leathers in Shanghai often express their opinions to the bureau and request the prompt initiation of inspection. After the preparation began, the bureau sent personnel to investigate and study the matter, drafted detailed inspection rules, and solicited the opinions of the trade association, hoping that both inspection policy and commercial conditions would be taken into consideration and that the handling would be perfect. On April 21st, a letter was sent to the association requesting them to send representatives to the bureau for a meeting to make a final decision. When the letter was sent, it was addressed to Mr. Lu Qinglai, Chairman of the Shanghai Hide, Leather, Oil, and Bone Trade Association, as the association's submissions were always signed by him. At the meeting, Mr. Lu and Mr. Yuan Meiqing attended, and their attitude during the discussion was very good. However, afterwards (the association suddenly sent a letter denying it), and the letter only bore the association's seal without the signature of a responsible person. How the truth is in this is very puzzling. The association asked the City Chamber of Commerce to telegraph the Ministry of Industry, claiming to represent the entire industry, but they don't know that there are also people in the industry who are requesting the implementation of inspection. Since the industry association has requested the City Chamber of Commerce to telegraph the Ministry of Industry, the bureau will naturally report the facts to the Ministry and await instructions.

City Chamber of Commerce Instructs That Payment Slips Should Bear Stamps 100

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce sent a letter yesterday to the Foil Industry Association, instructing that payment slips should bear stamps. [Beginning] Dear Sirs, We received your letter of the 13th of this month, requesting an explanation as to whether notification slips should bear stamps, and attached a sample to the association. Upon examination of the attached sample, it clearly states "Now sending you the sum of X yuan, and kindly acknowledge receipt for Shaoxing XX Company." This indicates that Sanhe Fubo Foil Company is using this slip to make payments, which is of the same nature as the payment slips mentioned in the remarks column of the fourth item of the stamp tax rate schedule. The person issuing the payment slip should affix the stamp. The letter states that the bank receiving the payment has a seal on the slip, which is in the nature of a receipt. This association believes that even as stated in the letter, it is a payment slip that also serves as a bank receipt. According to Article 8 of the Stamp Tax Law, if the tax rates are the same, only one type of stamp should be affixed. The payer issues the payment slip first, and the recipient seals it later. According to the provisions of Article 5 of the Implementing Rules of the Stamp Tax Law, the stamp tax ticket should be affixed to the document subject to stamp tax before it is delivered or used. Therefore, the foil company making the payment should affix sufficient stamps before delivering or using this payment slip. In any case, the responsibility cannot be shirked onto the person who seals the receipt.

Bank of China Research Office Revises National Bank Yearbook, Scheduled for Publication in September... Pre-Orders Now Being Accepted 103

The Economic Research Office of the Head Office of the Bank of China has been making unremitting efforts in economic research. The various books it has compiled have made many contributions to economic research. Previously, in view of the fact that China's banking industry lacked comprehensive and systematic records and statistics, it began compiling and printing the National Bank Yearbook in 1934. After its publication, it was widely praised by all sectors as the only reliable reference for studying the banking industry. After the second edition of the Yearbook was published last July, it resumed its work on the third survey and compilation, which took nearly a year to complete. The compilation method has also been greatly reformed, and efforts have been made to ensure that the inspection and application are accurate, complete, and convenient. The reporter, considering that this work is attracting attention from the financial community, specially visited the person in charge of the office. He was told that this is the third edition of the Yearbook since its publication. After the first two editions were published, corrections were sought from experts and banking authorities at home and abroad in order to be practical. They were generous with their advice, either praising excessively or providing detailed compilation guidelines and strict criticisms. The office studied them and made some additions to the second edition. This year, the survey method and compilation content were revised to meet the original intention of compiling the Yearbook. The main points of the revision are as follows: The Yearbook was originally divided into two parts, main and supplementary, with a total of sixteen chapters. The main part had ten chapters, which were purely records of Chinese-owned banks. The supplementary part had six chapters, which were records of financial institutions other than Chinese-owned banks, such as foreign banks, trust companies, savings associations, silver companies, money shops, pawnshops, and treasury houses. This year, in response to factual needs, attention was paid to the investigation of financial conditions in various places, so it was specially revised into three parts: upper, middle, and lower. The upper part is an overview, with ten chapters. The middle part is a financial survey of various places, with eight chapters. The lower part is statistics, laws, and regulations, and others, with six chapters, for a total of twenty-four chapters. The upper part, the overview, has a total of ten chapters: Chapter 1 is a chronicle of major banking events; Chapter 2 is on central and chartered banks; Chapter 3 is on provincial and municipal banks; Chapter 4 is on commercial banks; Chapter 5 is on savings banks; Chapter 6 is on agricultural and industrial banks; Chapter 7 is on specialized banks; Chapter 8 is on overseas Chinese banks; Chapter 9 is on foreign banks; Chapter 10 is on other financial institutions. Classification by category seems more reasonable and convenient for inspection. The middle part, the financial survey of various places, has a total of eight chapters: Chapter 11 is on the nine major cities; Chapter 12 is on East China; Chapter 13 is on North China; Chapter 14 is on Central China; Chapter 15 is on South China; Chapter 16 is on Northeast China; Chapter 17 is on Northwest China; Chapter 18 is on Hong Kong and abroad. A place name index is attached at the end of the chapter. The lower part, statistics, laws, and regulations, and others, has a total of six chapters: Chapter 19 is on banking statistics; Chapter 20 is on banking laws; Chapter 21 is on banking regulations; Chapter 22 is on banking annual reports; Chapter 23 is on banking logs; Chapter 24 is an index of banking treatises. The list of banking personnel in Chapter 7 of the original main part has been deleted completely because it has been scattered in various chapters and the data this year has increased significantly in order to save space. Those who have the first and second editions of the Yearbook are sufficient for inspection needs. The classification of Chinese-owned banks in the upper part is different from the previous two years. The previous two years were only statistical classifications, while this year is a compilation classification, and the convenience of consultation must be taken into account. Moreover, because the names and businesses of Chinese banks often do not match completely, the compilation and division are also very difficult. After comprehensive investigation of the characteristics of the names and businesses of various banks, they are divided as described in the first item. Secondly, the foreign bank part restores the national compilation method. The assets, liabilities, and profit and loss statements of each bank in the upper part were limited to one year in the first and second editions, that is, the number of 1934 was published in 1935, and the number of 1936 was published in 1937. Readers feel that this time distance seems too long, and there is a lack of a sense of satisfaction when consulting. The reason for this is that the settlement of accounts of each bank is not convenient for publication until after the meeting, and the timing varies, even after June or July each year; two, the issue is paid in March and April. It is printed in , makeup is not enough to publish the latest numbers, and now that the stock markets of the banks have been brought forward, the collection of the tables is easier, and this year it has been decided to publish the numbers for 1934 and 1935 to supplement the existing definite opinions. The publication time is therefore slightly delayed by thirty or forty days. The business statistics in Chapter 19, Banking Statistics, were also limited to one year. This year, all the numbers from 1932 to 1935 have been compiled separately for comparison. The banking regulations published in Chapter 21 are completely different from those published in the first and second editions, which readers can study. The publication of banking annual reports in Chapter 22 began in the second edition, so the original publication reached six years. Now, all annual reports of each bank in 1935 are published uniformly, and the number of banks has also increased. The local financial surveys in the previous two editions were generally communications and reports from the branches of the bank. However, in some important commercial and financial centers, the bank did not have any branches, so they were all missing. This year, since attention is paid to local financial surveys and it is not possible for the branches of the bank, it is not permitted to send personnel directly to investigate, so special letters are sent to colleagues who have branches to investigate on their behalf, but there are many difficulties in the full survey. , so first select more than thirty of the most important ones and send letters soliciting contributions as a test. Since March, except for one or two places, they have all provided detailed investigations and replies, which can be said to be a major gain in the content of the Yearbook. It is learned that the Yearbook is now being printed one after another and is scheduled for publication in September. Pre-orders are now being accepted, and in order to strive for popularization, the fixed price of eight yuan has been changed to six yuan, and the pre-order price of five yuan has been changed to four yuan, reducing the burden on readers by more than 20%.

Epidemic Prevention Campaign Begins Today; All Teams Mobilized for Inoculations in All Districts; Some Doctors Assigned to Inoculate at Hospitals; Ambulances Patrol and Are Stationed on All Roads 104

The city-wide epidemic prevention campaign, organized by the Municipal Health Bureau, is scheduled to begin today. All inoculation teams for preventive vaccinations have been ordered to mobilize. Ambulances patrol all roads, providing free inoculations for citizens. The Municipal Health Bureau has also issued a public notice to all citizens, warning against cholera. The details are as follows:

Inoculation Teams Fully Mobilized

The Shanghai South Clinic, Zhabei Clinic, Jiangwan Office, Wusong Health Office, Gaoqiao Health Office, and other health agencies responsible for cholera prevention, after receiving clear orders from the Municipal Health Bureau, have organized epidemic prevention inoculation teams from the doctors, technicians, male and female nurses, etc., originally at their respective clinics and offices. Except for a portion who remain on duty in the facilities, the rest, in groups of two to three, carrying vaccine needles, will all be mobilized starting at 9:00 AM today. They will go to various places to administer preventive inoculations. Each group will be led by a doctor or technician, and will work within the areas under their jurisdiction as stipulated by the Health Bureau.

Ambulances Patrol the Roads

In addition, more than ten patient ambulances from the clinics, offices, and the Municipal Health Bureau will patrol the roads in various districts from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM daily. They will stop in traffic hubs and places with high pedestrian traffic to administer compulsory vaccinations. If cases of cholera are discovered when necessary, they will be immediately rescued and sent to designated hospitals for treatment. At the same time, the concession authorities have also designated districts to be responsible for carrying out the campaign, it is said.

Health Bureau Public Notice

The Municipal Health Bureau issued a public notice to citizens, saying, "Summer has arrived, and it is again the time when cholera (medically called cholera) threatens people. Listen to the guidance of this bureau to avoid harm. Please implement the following measures, which are guaranteed to be beneficial and harmless: You should get a cholera vaccination. This bureau provides it free of charge. Flies easily carry cholera microbes. Do not eat anything that flies have landed on. Everyone should kill flies. Do not drink unboiled water, as it may contain cholera microbes. Do not carelessly eat cut fruits, or Holland water, ice cream, or sour plum juice made with raw water, to avoid bringing trouble into your stomach. Do not mingle with people who have cholera. Send people with cholera to the hospital immediately for treatment. If you feel even slightly unwell, see a doctor immediately. Do not pick at your skin or take medicine without consulting a doctor. Do not sleep outdoors. When sleeping, cover your abdomen with clothing or other items. Discharges from patients (vomit, feces) should be treated with lime water for one or two hours before being poured into the sewer. Do not pour them indiscriminately, as they contain invisible microbes that may still be alive and harm others. If everyone can diligently implement the above methods, cholera will have difficulty harming people. Regarding the matter of getting vaccinated, since you cannot do it yourself, this bureau will send people to do it for you. After the vaccination, your body will develop a resistance to cholera. If you do not encounter cholera microbes, you will naturally not get cholera. Even if you accidentally encounter cholera microbes, the illness can be mitigated. This bureau is helping you protect your health, and it does not cost you a penny. Why not come for vaccination soon? Now that it has been explained in detail, everyone please come quickly for vaccination. Each person should be vaccinated twice. After the vaccination, the injection site may be slightly swollen or painful, or you may feel slightly unwell. This is because your body has already developed resistance to cholera. It will be better in a day and will not be a problem. Please rest assured, and follow the guidance of this bureau to avoid the tragedy of getting cholera and losing your life. If you can help this bureau explain the above words to illiterate people, your merit will be great. Please implement it yourself, and advise everyone to get cholera vaccinations to avoid getting cholera. Everyone should get a vaccination before getting cholera, as it will be too late once you get cholera. Each person should get two injections. This bureau understands that workers are busy with their work and may not have time to take care of their own disease prevention methods, so this bureau will send people to various factories and groups to give injections free of charge. It is hoped that the staff and foremen of various factories will enthusiastically encourage this. This is not only your duty, but also a beautiful virtue of human benevolence and mutual assistance. Regarding this matter, it can be seen whether the managers, staff, and foremen of various factories are concerned about the health of the workers. If you truly care for the workers, you will surely enthusiastically encourage them, and the workers who get vaccinated will naturally be enthusiastic. It is hoped that the managers, staff, and foremen of various factories will pay more attention to the health of the workers and encourage them to get preventive vaccinations, which is of utmost importance. All citizens can go to the doctors or hospitals entrusted by this bureau near them to get cholera vaccinations (all have signs of various preventive vaccination locations hanging in front), free of charge. Also, for any gathering of thirty people, you can first report to this bureau, schedule a date for doctors to come for vaccination, also free of charge. This bureau is completely maintaining the health of our citizens, preventing the harm of cholera, hoping that everyone will accept the advice and get cholera vaccinations. In addition, everyone should also pay attention to hygiene."

Zhejiang Province's Method of Storing Fuel for Steamships; Shipping Merchants Unanimously Oppose 105

The 1st District Ship Management Office of Zhejiang Province recently drafted a method for steamship merchants to store fuel, along with an appended guarantee, using administrative power to force shipping merchants to sign and acknowledge it. The Shanghai Inland River Steamship Industry Association, after receiving reports from its members, has already telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction, requesting that they take into consideration the difficulties of merchants and exempt them from storing fuel. This has been reported in previous newspapers. According to reliable news from the inland river shipping industry, since the Ship Management Office of the district announced the above-mentioned storage method, shipping merchants in Huzhou, Pinghu, and other counties under its jurisdiction have been greatly alarmed. Regarding the matter of being forced to sign the guarantee, they believe it is an insult to the dignity of shipping merchants. Public sentiment is very indignant. If the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction does not provide proper relief for the aforementioned method, various shipping merchants operating in Zhejiang Province will be summoned to Shanghai in the future to hold a meeting to discuss effective countermeasures. Their attitude is extremely intense, it is said.

After the murder of Japanese woman Marumoto Kamemaru, a tenant in the upstairs room of Chen Hongyuan's tobacco, alcohol, and grocery store at No. 279 Miller Road in Hongkou, was discovered on March 3, following a strict investigation by the Japanese police station, the perpetrator of the case, Tanaka Hidesaburo, was arrested on April 19 on Seward Road and taken back to the Japanese police station for interrogation. It is now known that the cause of the case was a dispute over solicitation of nighttime entertainment expenses. At the same time, the evidence of the crime was conclusive and could not be denied. Therefore, Tanaka Hidesaburo also confessed. Bandit Wang Rongfu; Attempts Suicide Out of Fear of Punishment, Fails 110

At the Sande Tea House on Zhongshan Road in Zhabei, at around 9:30 PM on April 11, traces of burglary were discovered. Patrol Officer Li Yiqian and Sergeant Fu Yongkang of the Baziqiao Police Station led a large number of police officers to arrest the burglars. They engaged the bandits, exchanging fire for twenty to thirty rounds. One bandit was shot. The bandits were outnumbered, and Dong Jingzhai, Qi Defu, Xiao Fulong, and Jiao Furong were arrested on the spot. A six-round automatic pistol and four bullets were seized. Two unexploded grenades released by the bandits were found. Subsequently, another bandit, Zhao Debiao, and his mistress, Bu Sanyuan, were apprehended. A Mauser pistol bullet was also found. Bandit leader Li Shouheng, who was the squad leader of the Pengpu District Defense Corps, escaped after the incident. The details of his arrest and delivery to the bureau for interrogation by the Defense Corps have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that one of the bandits shot was Wang Rongfu, a native of Funing, 29 years old, who was shot five times, once in the neck and twice in each leg. He was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. After more than twenty days, his injuries gradually healed. Unexpectedly, the bandit Wang, fearing punishment, took advantage of the lack of supervision the day before yesterday in the deep of night, and used a piece of broken lead skin bowl to cut his genitals in an attempt to commit suicide. He was discovered bleeding from his wounds. The Public Security Bureau, upon hearing this, ordered Liang Fuchu, the chief of the North Station Branch, and Gu Liancheng and Guo Mengqu, the leaders of the Investigation Detachment, to dispatch investigators Kong Rongsheng and Hu Daoxi to the hospital at 5:30 PM the day before yesterday, together with Western Detective McCutcheon and Chinese Detective Pang Qing of the Laoza Police Station, to take the bandit Wang into custody for interrogation by the Investigation General Team.

Husband's Physiological Defect; Wife Petitions for Divorce; Court Mediation Failed Yesterday 111

Li Yueying, a woman from Hangzhou, 23 years old, currently residing at No. 58 Zhuangjia Lane, Ximen, recently engaged a lawyer to file a petition with the Civil Division of the Special No. 2 Court, requesting mediation for divorce from her husband, Hu Hongxing, from Anhui (who works at the Yutai Tea House's main branch on Foch Road). The petition stated that she married the defendant in October of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Initially, their marriage was harmonious, but she later learned that the defendant had a physiological defect and could not fulfill their marital obligations. The petitioner, mindful of the fact that her parents had passed away early and her adoptive father had moved far away, endured this and did not complain. Unexpectedly, the defendant had ill intentions and gradually became indifferent to the petitioner, developing a feeling of disgust, and eventually treating her as an enemy. The petitioner, in this situation, felt that life was unbearable. Later, through the mediation of Cao Boqing, the defendant was ordered to transfer all his savings of a little over eight hundred yuan to the petitioner's name in April of the 24th year of the Republic of China for monthly interest payments, and the defendant would pay a monthly living expense of seven yuan until December of the 24th year of the Republic of China. The defendant returned to Anhui alone. Two months later, he sent a letter to his sister, Pinlan, expressing his desire to divorce the petitioner. Upon learning this, the petitioner, feeling that her future was uncertain and suffering mentally and economically, attempted suicide by drowning herself in the Dongmen Road Bund on February 14 of the 25th year of the Republic of China. She was rescued, taken to the Public Security Bureau, and sent back home. However, after this incident, the defendant still did not repent and stopped paying the monthly allowance, and regarded the petitioner with animosity, vowing to divorce. Since the defendant had expressed his determination, the petitioner had no choice but to petition for mediation for divorce, etc. The court granted the request, and yesterday morning, Judge Guo Wei presided over the mediation in the Civil Division 4. Both parties appeared in court as summoned. First, the petitioner, Li Yueying, stated the intent of her petition for mediation. Then, the defendant, Hu Hongxing, was asked if he agreed to the divorce, and he said that he could agree to the divorce, but as a merchant, he only had the amount of savings previously given, and asked the petitioner to return some of it. Li Yueying said that the savings of a little over eight hundred yuan were not enough to cover living expenses, and that the defendant should allocate more funds, etc. After repeated persuasion by the judge, the two parties refused to yield. The court then announced that the mediation had failed and ordered a formal lawsuit.

Lawyer Wen Ren'an; Has a Major Conflict with Defendant; A Disturbance in the Case of Petition for Separate Residence 112

Yesterday afternoon at 2:25 PM, lawyer Wen Ren'an appeared in the First Special District Court representing his client, Lin Lingdi, a woman from Ningbo, in a case of petition for separate residence from her husband, Zhang Yongshan, from Ningbo. It is unknown how, but he suddenly had a major argument with Zhang Yongshan, and then they began to fight each other outside the door of Court 14. Lawyer Wen's glasses were also knocked to the ground. The details are as follows: Zhang Yongshan has been working at Eurasia Aviation Company. In May of the year before last, he met Lin Lingdi, a woman from Ningbo. Their friendship developed into love, and eventually they had a physical relationship. After a considerable amount of time, as their feelings reached a boiling point, they asked a matchmaker to arrange a marriage. They formally married at a restaurant on Wuma Road on the 21st day of the first month of the Lunar New Year last year. During the wedding ceremony, because Lin Lingdi was already pregnant, she gave birth to a son on May 29, just a few months later. Unexpectedly, a rift suddenly appeared between the couple after one year of marriage. Recently, Lin Lingdi, unable to bear her husband's abuse, hired lawyer Wen Ren'an to file a petition with the Civil Division of the First Special District Court, requesting separation from her husband, Zhang Yongshan, and the return of her jewelry. This case has already been summoned once, ordering them to attempt reconciliation outside the court. Yesterday afternoon, it was time for the continued hearing. Therefore, both plaintiffs and defendants arrived in court with their lawyers. Unexpectedly, before the trial began, Zhang Yongshan and lawyer Wen Ren'an suddenly had a conflict. Lawyer Wen pointed at Zhang and began to scold him, and then they began to fight, wrestling together. Court police officers arrived to separate them and led both parties to the judicial police station to state what happened. Because the matter was minor and neither party had suffered any serious injuries, they were ordered to leave and file their own lawsuits. Shortly after, Judge Huang Risheng presided over the interrogation in Civil Division 12. The plaintiff, Lin Lingdi, immediately submitted a case, stating that she was unable to reconcile during the adjournment because she had been married to the defendant, and her jewelry and clothes had been pawned. All of her private savings of three thousand yuan had also been used up, disregarding her family's needs. If she did not agree, she would be beaten and kicked repeatedly. She was unable to bear the pain and sincerely requested permission for separate residence, vowing not to return home, etc. Then, the plaintiff's representative, lawyer Wen, recounted in court the incident of being beaten by Zhang a moment ago, stating that the defendant was extremely barbaric. Not only did he abuse his wife, but he also insulted and humiliated this lawyer, who had never met him before. His usual behavior was self-evident, etc. When Zhang Yongshan was questioned, he completely denied the plaintiff's accusations, saying that his relationship with Lin Lingdi was always harmonious, requesting the dismissal of the lawsuit, and filing a counterclaim, requesting a judgment ordering them to live together. Judge Huang announced the conclusion of the debate on this case and scheduled the verdict to be announced at 1:00 PM on the 19th.

Female Student; Commits Suicide Due to Sadness Over Her Circumstances; Academic Failure and Financial Distress; Commits Suicide by Taking Sleeping Pills 113

Zeng Guan'e, a Cantonese woman, 23 years old, residing at No. 28 Xiangyu Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei, is currently studying obstetrics under Dr. He Xiuzhen, and has been studying for only eight months. Zeng's family is poor. Unexpectedly, the woman suddenly worried that her studies were not progressing and that she was experiencing financial difficulties, and she became weary of the world. Alone, she went to Room 281 of the Delin Apartment on Chongming Road, wrote a suicide note stating the reason for her suicide and the location, and sent it to her cousin, Zeng Wenbiao. Then, she secretly swallowed sleeping pills and committed suicide. When Wenbiao received her letter the day before yesterday at noon, he immediately went to the woman's home to inform her. Together with the woman's brother, Zeng Wangyao, they went to the inn and found the woman groaning on the bed. They urgently called an ambulance to the scene and rushed her to Shanghai Sanatorium and Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective. She died the day before yesterday. The Hongkou Police Station, upon receiving the report, ordered Chinese Detective Chen Xikang to go to the scene for investigation. He then carried the body to the Fei Lun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Zhang Zongru, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, accompanied by forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, went to the morgue to examine the body. According to the report of Chinese Police Chief Zhang Yuhai, Zhang confirmed that the deceased female student, Zeng Guan'e, had indeed committed suicide by taking sleeping pills. The corpse was handed over to her brother, Zeng Wangyao, for coffin preparation and burial.

New Traffic Methods Implemented at the Intersection of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road Yesterday 114

The Public Concession’s Public Works Department has recently paid close attention to the safety of vehicles and pedestrians on the roads. In addition to the intersections of Weihaiwei Road and Seymour Road, and Avenue Road and Jiaozhou Road, where new traffic methods have been implemented, the tram stop at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road was reformed yesterday, moving the stop near Jing’an Temple Road by more than ten feet and the one near Nanjing Road by two feet, so as to enlarge the area at the road intersection to facilitate vehicles turning. On the other hand, wooden posts have also been nailed to the pavement at the four corners, with cables added to them, so that pedestrians who want to cross the road can cross the road farther away from the intersection. This is of great convenience to both motorists and pedestrians.

Japanese Sailors; Were Stopped Yesterday While Passing Through the French Concession; Because They Did Not Have a Transit Permit 115

According to the Da Mei Evening News, this morning (the 14th) at 9:30 AM, four trucks carrying Japanese marines departed from Hongkou for a tour of the city. They were led by several officers in a military vehicle. When they drove along Sichuan Road and passed Avenue Edward, as they were about to enter Rue du Consulat in the French Concession, they were stopped by an Annamese constable because the Japanese soldiers did not have a transit permit issued by the French Police Station and were not allowed to enter the concession. For a time, onlookers surrounded them like a wall, and traffic was blocked. Later, the Japanese officer called the French Police Station. After waiting for a long time, a French constable came with the permit, and they were finally able to drive to the Chinese territory. Because they had obtained a Chinese permit in advance, they did not encounter any obstacles when entering Chinese territory.

Donghua Coal Mining Company Directors, Supervisors, Etc.; Trial Opens for Coal Sales Commission Lawsuit; Creditors File Suit to Declare Two Commission Agreements Invalid in Order to Maintain Their Own Interests; Defendants Claim Plaintiffs Have No Right to Sue 117

The Jia Wang Coal Mining Company had previously accumulated a large amount of debt to shorthand and other households, making it difficult to maintain operations. The company was reorganized into the China East Coal Mining Company Limited. The creditor rights of Jia Wang's creditors were also subject to a repayment plan. After China East continued to operate, in order to raise funds to develop new coal mines, it negotiated with Liu Hongsheng to borrow 800,000 yuan. In addition to mortgaging the new mine and paying interest monthly, it also agreed that for every ton of coal sold from the new mine,

A Commission of Thirty Cents

But that loan was not established, and the commission agreement was only reduced from thirty cents to twenty cents. However, Gu did not raise the funds, and the planned projects were not all completed. However, for the commission agreement, although some directors and supervisors opposed it, they did not agree to cancel it. As a result, internal

Illegal Commission

agreement was invalid in order to avoid damage to creditors' interests. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Tao Dejun opened the court for trial. The Major Criminal in a Murder Case That Lasted Over Six Years Was Finally Arrested: Liu Liuguanzi Could Not Escape the Law and Was Detained Awaiting Sentencing; Wang Tingzhang Narrated the Circumstances of the Shooting to Avenge His Brother 119

Wang Baosan from Funing used to handle affairs at a cleaning station in Zhabei before 1930. Due to a dispute over the profits from foul manure with Dai Ruzhao and his disciples Wang Fugang, Shi Fulin, and Liu Liuguanzi (also known as Liu Xingsan), Wang Baosan was shot to death by a barrage of gunfire on the afternoon of February 28, 1930. The Municipal Public Security Bureau successively arrested Dai Ruzhao, Wang Fugang, and Shi Fulin, and handed them over to the Shanghai Local Court for trial. According to the old criminal law for premeditated murder, Dai Ruzhao was sentenced to death, Wang Fugang to life imprisonment, and Shi Fulin to twelve years of imprisonment. Subsequently, the three defendants appealed to the Suzhou High Court, and the three-instance trial concluded with the original sentences upheld. Dai Ruzhao was executed by hanging in the Suzhou prison on June 1 of last year. Wang Fugang and Shi Fulin also died in prison one after another. Liu Liuguanzi, who had been on the run, initially fled elsewhere, but now, believing that time had passed and things had changed, he returned to Shanghai and lived with his wife in the home of his disciple Wu Xiaokaizi on Hankow Road in the Hongqiao area. However, Wang Baosan's wife, Wang Shi, had also passed away. Liu thought he was safe, but unexpectedly, his younger brother Wang Tingzhang learned of his situation. He entrusted people to investigate, and Liu gradually realized that he was being investigated and wanted to leave Shanghai again. He borrowed 20 yuan from Wu Xiaokaizi for travel expenses. Wu declined, saying that he was just a small worker and had no spare money. Liu became furious and threatened Wu, saying that if he did not lend the money, there would be days of crying. No more than three days after he said this, Wu Xiaokaizi's wife went missing. Wu, believing that Liu's threat had a hidden meaning and that he was clearly suspicious, told a friend who was a civil servant about the matter, seeking justice. His friend drafted a written statement detailing the circumstances and planned to file a complaint. He immediately handed Liu Liuguanzi over to the local police station. Because the written statement stated that Liu was a fugitive murderer, he was transferred to the Zhabei Police Station, which presented him to the Public Security Bureau and transferred him to the Local Court for detention. Wang Tingzhang also filed a lawsuit. The prosecutor filed a public prosecution, and Zhao Yongzhou, the judge, opened the trial yesterday morning. Liu Liuguanzi claimed that he was not called Liu Liuguanzi, but his original name was Liu Xingsan, and he knew nothing about the Wang Baosan case. The judge questioned him, saying that Wang Shi had provided very detailed testimony before, so how could he deny it? However, Liu insisted on denying everything. Subsequently, the witnesses Xue Ziying, Dai Xiazhang, Ji Shangwen, and Lu Xiaogouzi all testified that the defendant was indeed Liu Liuguanzi. The defendant's witnesses, Bi Changsheng, Tang Baofu, and Dai Chunshan, testified that the defendant was not Liu Liuguanzi, but his real name was Liu Xingsan. Finally, Wang Tingzhang, the brother of the deceased, testified that he lived at 9 Tianbao Road, was from Yancheng, and his sister-in-law was dead. He said that Dai Ruzhao fired two shots at his brother's death, Wang Fugang fired one shot, and Liu Liuguanzi was the most vicious, firing a total of four shots. At this point, Prosecutor Xie argued that the facts were very clear and there was no room for denial, and requested that he be sentenced according to law. The judge then declared the debate closed and scheduled the sentencing announcement for 2 PM on the 20th of this month. The defendant was returned to custody.

Dalu News reports that French poet and novelist Jean Cocteau has recently reached an agreement with Le Journal to travel around the world in 80 days. During the journey, he is not allowed to travel by airplane, airship, or balloon. His return to Paris must not be earlier or later than 80 days. On the 80th day, Le Journal will welcome him at the train station. If he fulfills the agreement by midnight on that day, Le Journal will pay for his travel expenses and his稿费. Narcotics Found on Worker: 56 People Willing to Vouch for Him, Proving His Honest Character and that He Was Framed: Hearing Postponed for 7 Days to Ascertain the Facts 132

Lin Yunfu, a worker from Huzhou at the Meiwen Wire Mesh Factory at No. 15, Lane 645, Xichangping Road, was arrested suddenly near Changping Road and Zhedelu at 5:05 AM the day before yesterday by two Chinese constables No. 674 and No. 1986 on suspicion. A package of heroin was found in his pocket and he was taken to the Gordon Road Police Station. Under questioning by Chinese and foreign detectives, and at the house of Zheng at No. 359, Lane 67, Xiaoshadu Road, 4 packages of heroin (each containing 10 small packages) and 7 pounds of white powder resembling baking soda were found, and were taken to the police station and impounded. Yesterday morning, he was transferred to the 8th Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The Municipal Council charged him under Article 257 of the Criminal Code with the crime of selling and transporting opium, or under Article 263 of the same law with the crime of possessing opium. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, rose to state the case, saying that the white powder and 20 grams of heroin found on the defendant and at his home had been sent to the Municipal Council's Health Bureau for chemical testing. The results have not yet been received, so a postponement was requested. However, the defendant stated at the police station that he denied having the narcotics and that he was framed by others. However, when the defendant was arrested, a park pass was found on his person, so the police suspected that the defendant may have been selling the narcotics in the park, etc. In conclusion, the defendant Zheng Lianfu stated that he was indeed framed in this matter. A fellow villager named Zhang Cai, who is addicted to drugs, often stayed at my place when he came to Shanghai. On the 10th and 12th of this month, he borrowed money from me twice without success and left unhappily, so I suspect he framed me. I myself suffer from lung disease, so every morning at 5:00 AM, I have to go to Jiaozhou Road Park to practice Tai Chi. The blue cloth clothes I wear for work are full of stains, and I am afraid of being refused entry to the park, so I wear black shorts and shirts instead. The shorts and shirts are hung on the wall at home and the enemy can plot against me at any time, etc. Finally, the defendant's defense lawyer, Shi Liang, stated that the defendant has worked at the Meiwen Silk Factory for nine years, and his conduct has always been honest and he is deeply trusted by his colleagues in the factory. He has been framed this time, so 56 workers from the same factory have come to court today and are willing to vouch for him. She requested that bail be granted. Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the confession and ordered that the case be postponed for seven days for further investigation. The defendant was ordered to be detained at the Huade Road Tilanqiao Prison.

Shin Hsin No. 9 Factory's Appeal Against Municipal General Tax Rejected: Supreme Court Upholds the Principle of the First Instance 133

The Shin Hsin Textile No. 9 Factory at No. 140 Macau Road in this port owed the Municipal General Tax of 11,900 yuan to the Municipal Council's Tax Office. The Municipal Council filed a lawsuit in the First Special District Court. As a result, the defendant was defeated and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, but the appeal was also rejected. Shin Hsin No. 9 Factory then appealed to the Supreme Court, raising two points: 1. 15% of the factory's existing unused houses should no longer be subject to housing tax. 2. The market is depressed, and the housing tax should be reduced by 15% as an example. The Supreme Court has now ruled to reject the appeal, because the vacant houses can be used at any time and are different from those with separate and independent door numbers. Furthermore, the initial valuation of the factory's houses was 255,500 yuan, which was later reduced to 170,000 yuan. It has not been long since then, and there has been no major change in the prosperity or decline of the market. It is difficult to make a strong comparison with houses that have not previously received reduced valuation benefits. Moreover, whether or not the housing tax should be reduced, unless it has been agreed or judged by the changing party, the appeal cannot be made unilaterally. Therefore, the appeal was deemed unreasonable and the original judgment of the first instance should be upheld. It is noted that this case was initially filed in October of last year, and was ruled by the Supreme Court at the end of last month, which took more than half a year.

The total amount is 5 million yuan.

The Mongu Road Police Station; Police Chief Has Illicit Affair with Married Woman 140

Li Haifeng Embezzles Public Funds and Flees; Jiang Dongbao Accidentally Discovers Secret Letter

Jiang Dongbao, 42 years old, a native of Ningbo, lived at 9 Dongjunji Lane, Xinjiang Road, Zhabei, where he made a living by running a small book stall at the entrance of the lane. He married Ms. Chen (named Qiaoying) over ten years ago. Ms. Chen had three sons, the eldest named Pinshan, already 12 years old. Unexpectedly, Ms. Chen was recently seduced into an affair by Li Haifeng, the chief of the Mongu Road Police Station. The police chief is also married, so there have been several domestic disputes. Although Jiang knew about it, he feared Li's power as a police officer and was concerned about his reputation, so he did not dare to speak out and had no recourse. Unexpectedly, at the end of last month, Li Haifeng instigated Qiaoying to take their six-year-old youngest son and flee. Li himself also abandoned his post and fled. Initially, he went to the home of his friend Xu Dekui in Nanjing. Xu is a police officer in the Nanjing Public Security Bureau. Later, Xu had business in Shanghai, and Li Haifeng took Qiaoying and others back to the Qingleju Hotel at the Zhenjiang West Station to stay temporarily. He then entrusted Xu to bring a letter to Qiaoying's mother in Shanghai on the 10th of this month. The letter contained ten dollars. Because Qiaoying's mother was illiterate, she took the letter to a nearby letter reader to read it. By chance, Jiang Dongbao happened to see it. Jiang snatched the letter and found that it asked his mother to find a way to trick the eldest and second sons out and send them to Zhenjiang, and instructed her not to let Dongbao know. At this point, Jiang could no longer bear it. That night, he took a letter and went to the Mongu Road Police Station to request an investigation. The Police Chief Li Ducha was already aware that Police Chief Li Haifeng had embezzled over 120 yuan in public funds and fled. He had already reported it to the Public Security Bureau and issued an arrest warrant, but did not know where the police chief had gone. After hearing the report, Police Chief Li learned that the police chief had not only embezzled public funds, but also abducted a married woman. He secretly dispatched Internal Affairs Police Chief Rong Faxi and Investigator Sun Youyi. The next day, carrying official documents, they took the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway train to Zhenjiang Station. As the investigators got off the train, it was raining. Li Haifeng was already waiting at the station. Qiaoying's mother, Police Chief Rong, and Investigator Sun, knowing Li Haifeng, got off the train and arrested him. They then cooperated with the police of the Second Branch of the Fifth Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau and rushed to the Qingleju Hotel, arresting Qiaoying and the child. They took the train back to Shanghai. Police Chief Li immediately summoned Jiang Dongbao and others. Jiang stated that he was busy with business and making a living, and had no time to litigate. He was willing to take Ms. Chen and her children back under his care. Qiaoying said that she was willing to repent and return home with her husband. Police Chief Li approved his request. However, the police chief had embezzled public funds and fled, and also dared to seduce and harbor a married woman. He was knowingly violating the law and had no regard for the law. He immediately prepared a document submitting the illegal police chief Li Haifeng to the Public Security Bureau for severe punishment, in order to maintain police discipline.

Representatives from various district branches, including Jiang, Gong Jingyan, Yu Shunfa, Chen Youqin, Wu Guowei, and Hu Zifang, etc., were also present. Ye Ruiqi, Cen Zhiliang, and Gu Wensheng were elected as the presidium. Tong Zhang served as the master of ceremonies, and Yu Jingqing recorded the minutes. After performing the rituals, Chairman Ye Ruiqi delivered the opening speech. Cen Zhiliang reported on the progress of the work. Then, the representatives from the Party Headquarters and the General Federation of the Municipalities successively gave speeches. The following proposals were then discussed:

* A proposal to request the French authorities to increase the number of Chinese directors' seats based on the proportion of Chinese taxpayers within the concession. Resolved: Passed.

* A proposal to petition the Legislative Yuan to expedite the review of the mediation method for housing rent disputes promulgated and implemented by the Executive Yuan. Resolved: Passed.

* A proposal to request the French authorities to assess land prices fairly to facilitate rent reduction. Resolved: Passed.

* A proposal to notify citizens to uniformly ban smoking and reject drugs. Resolved: Passed.

* A proposal to oppose telephone price increases. Resolved: Unanimously opposed, and a letter will be sent to the telephone issue committee to actively negotiate.

* A proposal to address the French Police Department's indiscriminate copying of store doorplates and unwarranted penalties, requiring effective negotiation. Resolved: To be submitted to the Executive Committee to formulate detailed measures and be responsible for negotiation.

* The review fees for classified business licenses collected by the French Concession are unaffordable and should be canceled, and the articles of association should be amended.

* Please negotiate with the French Municipal Council not to use the suspension of water and electricity supply as a means of increasing donations, and should proceed through legal procedures.

* Urge the Chinese directors to fulfill their duties. All proposals discussed by the directors' committees in the future should be reviewed by the General Tax Association before being discussed. The above three proposals were resolved and submitted to the Taxpayers' Association together, and letters were sent to all districts to advocate unanimously.

* A proposal to negotiate regarding the French water and electricity company's requirement that new users bear the previous users' arrears, and the use of suspension of water and electricity supply as a means of coercing payment. Resolved: A letter will be sent to the French Municipal Council for correction.

* A proposal to actively oppose the French water and electricity company's increase in deposit fees, which increases the burden on citizens. Resolved: Opposed, and the Executive Committee will formulate detailed measures.

* Organize a recruitment team to expand membership. Please discuss the drafting method. Resolved: The proposal was approved. The Executive Committee will issue letters of appointment to the captain and all team leaders before announcing the event. Temporary motions:

* Sun Shengchang, secretary of the Yongyuli Branch, requested that the owner be warned to reduce rent and requested assistance. Resolved: Assistance will be granted, and the owner will be warned to reduce rent voluntarily.

* Member He Yaozhang proposed that from now on, all cases of citizens within the district appealing to the French Concession Taxpayers' Association should be forwarded by the association, otherwise they will not be accepted. Resolved: A letter will be sent to the Taxpayers' Association for processing. After the discussion of the above cases, the executive committee was re-elected. As a result, Ye Ruiqi, Xu Xiuting, Dong Wenguansi, Cen Zhiliang, Dong Kechang, Huang Zhixian, Tong Lizhang, Shen Xibin, Xia Shanxiao, Gu Wensheng, Zhang Youmin, He Yaozhang, Zheng Ziliang, Ge Zizhan, Zhu Ding, Jin Mixieqi, and Cheng Yueting and 17 others were elected as executive committee members. Deng Guang, Gu Youyu, Qian Huimin, Feng Chengzhu, and Sun Wenchang, and 5 others were elected as alternate executive committee members. Finally, Chairman Wen Gusheng delivered the closing speech and the meeting was adjourned with refreshments.

Publishing World 148

"The Pyrethrum Industry" Book Has Been Published: The cultivation of pyrethrum is a profitable emerging agricultural crop. The manufacture of pyrethrum is an auspicious industry with light burdens and heavy profits. This has been generally recognized by the people of the country. Although its cultivation is quite simple, it is still difficult to harvest a good yield if the methods are not correct. The manufacturing method has always been kept secret by industrialists, and outsiders have no way of knowing it. Moreover, our country's mosquito coil manufacturing method uses the old method, and the productivity is not high, so it cannot compete with Japan in the world market. It is urgent to study and improve it. Mr. Shi Gongshan of Shanghai has done considerable research in this field. The "Pyrethrum Industry" book he wrote, in addition to detailing the methods of cultivation and reproduction, also publicly discloses the manufacturing secrets of mosquito coils, flea powder, fly powder, mosquito killing powder, and various agricultural insecticides. It introduces new Japanese and American manufacturing, equipment, machinery, and technology, which is truly the only reference book for increasing production efficiency and improving product quality. Domestic celebrities and scholars such as Sun Ke, Ye Chucang, Chen Gongbo, and Tang Zhicai have all inscribed and praised it, promoting it as a great help to the revival of China's agricultural and industrial economy. It is reported that it has been published by the World Book Bureau, priced at only seven cents.

"Chou Mou Monthly" Volume 2, Issue 9 Published: The ninth issue of the second volume of "Chou Mou Monthly" was published today (the 15th). The content is more exciting than before. Key articles include Gu Dizao's "Recent Events of the Past Month," Wei Youpei's "The Current Stage and Political Role of Smuggling in North China," Yang Gonghuai's "Prospects for German Foreign Development," Zhang Jiake's "How to Balance International Trade," Song Shushi's "Re-examination of Sino-Japanese Trade Relations," Yang Weiyu's "My Country's Contributions," Pan Yangyao's "A Word on Youth Cultivation," Li Wenjie's "Family Economic Issues," Wei Jin's translation of "Passionate Poet Byron," Qin Wen's "Wulin Travel," Wang Renshu's "The Last of the Fallen," Yang Jinhao's "Record of Xuanwu Lake," Shen Quji's "Que Shop," and Ding Kemei's "The Lost." A new column, "Art World," has been added, specializing in articles on film and drama. This issue is a "Special Page on the China Touring Theatre to Shanghai," with Zhao Jingshen's "On Oil Paint Not Dry," Wu Chengda's "Evaluation of La Traviata," Qian Taisheng's "Performance of Thunderstorm," and Yin Qinyi's "Mei Luoxiang." The retail price of each issue of the magazine is one dime. The special large edition will not be more expensive, and a copy of "Jiande Song Collection" compiled by Li Jinhui will be given away as a special offer. The distribution locations are the savings department of the Silk Industry Bank on Hankou Road, Shanghai, as well as branches and major bookstores.

Weather Report 149

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky around Shandong was cloudy with variable winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River and Hankou were changing from overcast to cloudy with morning fog and light unstable winds. The East China Sea and Taiwan were overcast with fog and gentle northeast to southeast winds. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was 67.1 degrees at its highest and 60.3 degrees at its lowest. On the same day last year, the temperature was 79.0 degrees at its highest and 63.0 degrees at its lowest.

The Eighth Annual Shanghai Elementary School Joint Sports Meet Opens Yesterday; Mayor Wu and Director Pan Attend and Deliver Speeches; Wang Yechao Sets New Record in Boys' Group C Shot Put; Excellent Results in Boys' Group B 200-Meter Preliminary Round 150

The eighth annual Shanghai Elementary School Joint Sports Meet opened yesterday at the Municipal Central District Stadium. Fortunately, the weather held, and all events were able to proceed smoothly. Details are as follows:

The Scene

Although the weather was overcast yesterday, nearly ten thousand students from various schools attended to watch. Although the scale of the organizing committee was small, all procedures followed those of the National Games. Therefore, the order at the venue was well-maintained. Flags from various schools fluttered in the air, their different colors quite vibrant and eye-catching. The Municipal Health Bureau specially dispatched doctors to provide first aid. The command platform was equipped with a megaphone, making all announcements clearly audible throughout the venue. Over twenty people, including Zhou Feicheng, Ma Chonggan, Shao Rugan, section chiefs Chen Bai and Mi Jifang, and Yuan Zengyu and Ding Shoutang from the Education Bureau, were present to handle hospitality matters.

Opening Ceremony

The opening ceremony took place at 10:00 AM. Mayor Wu, Director Pan, Municipal Secretary Zhang Tingrong, organizing committee chairman and vice-chairman Chen Bai, Ma Chonggan, Shao Rugan, Jiang Jianbai, and Zhang Yongchun, as well as referees Wang Fudan, Lin Yunsheng, and Li Jiyuan, and all the athletes, first marched around the field. After the music played and the flag was raised, a moment of silence was observed for three minutes in memory of the late Chairman of the Central Executive Committee, Hu Hanmin. Then, Chairman Mayor Wu delivered the opening address, followed by a report from Chen Bai, the organizing committee chairman. After all the athletes took their oaths, Lin Meiyan, the representative from the Municipal Party Committee, and Pan, the Director of the Education Bureau, delivered speeches. This was followed by group exercises.

Mayor's Speech

Mayor Wu delivered the opening address, saying, "Dear students, today is the eighth annual Shanghai Elementary School Joint Sports Meet. This is the first time our Shanghai Elementary School Joint Sports Meet has been held at the Shanghai Central District Stadium. The reason Shanghai built such a large stadium and invited the National Games to be held in Shanghai last year was to promote sports in Shanghai, to awaken Shanghai society's attention to sports, and especially to awaken our parents' attention to children's sports. Elementary school is the foundation of national education, and physical education is about strengthening our bodies and making our minds and bodies healthy. Therefore, physical education is the foundation of education. If our physical constitution is not healthy or developed, then our foundation is not solid. On an unsound foundation, no endeavor can be firmly established. The foundation of a person is their physique. With a developed physique and a healthy mind and body, the education one receives will allow one to succeed in their future service to society. This is true for individuals, and for the nation, it is true that if everyone has a developed physique, the foundation of the people is consolidated, which is the foundation for building the nation and reviving the nation. Therefore, the Shanghai Municipal Government built this great stadium and invited the National Games to be held here last year, with the aim of actively promoting sports and awakening society's attention to sports. I hope that the achievements of the eighth Elementary School Joint Sports Meet will be better than the previous one. These are a few words of encouragement that I want to give to all the athletes and elementary school students at today's opening ceremony."

Director Pan's Speech

Following speeches by Chen Bai and Lin Meiyan, Director Pan said, in brief, "The physical fitness of elementary school students must be cultivated in schools and families on a daily basis and cannot be interrupted for even one day. The purpose of this training is not just for holding sports meets but to serve the country and the nation. The meaning of the sports meet is simply to showcase the results of daily physical training, to compete with each other, and to seek progress. In fact, every elementary school student, whether an athlete or not, should train their bodies. The meaning of the sports meet is not only to encourage everyone to pay attention to physical training but also to pay attention to the order of the venue, the discipline of the event, and sportsmanship. Everyone must abide by order and discipline, so that during the three days of the event, no school or student will engage in undisciplined or unethical behavior. Only then will the sports meet be a success. Therefore, in addition to physical training, the morality of group living must also be cultivated here."

Parade and Oath

At 9:30 AM, the opening was announced. Athletes from each district, in the prescribed order, with the Hu Nan District leading and the Zhong Yin District at the rear, led by the Public Security Bureau Military Band, with bright flags and spirited military bearing, marched around the field to the sound of music. They then gathered in front of the command platform to take the oath. Luo Shouxuan from the First District of Hu Nan represented all the athletes in taking the oath: "We hereby adhere to the spirit of promoting physical education advocated by the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, participate in the competition as amateur athletes, obey the referees, and abide by all the rules of the event. This we swear."

Drill Performance

After the opening ceremony, three thousand elementary school students from various schools, all dressed in white uniforms, with the shorter ones in front and the taller ones in the back, entered the field one after another, led by their respective team leaders. They first paraded around the field for a week and then stood on the symbols indicating their positions according to the prescribed arrangement. Shao Rugan commanded the exercises, and the movements of the elementary school students were uniform and their steps were neat, earning applause from Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and all the guests. At the end of the exercises, they shouted "Long Live the Republic of China" three times, their patriotic spirit spontaneously arising, making it one of the most exciting scenes of the event.

Group Performances

Yesterday, the various schools put on over fifty group exercise performances. Among them, the German-style calisthenics of Wan Zhu, the Gong Lu boxing of He An, the dumbbell exercises of Si Shang, the "Baby Soldiers" of Cheng Dong, the walking imitation exercises of Yang Zheng, the fitness exercises of Mei Xi, the "Little Soldiers" of Shanghai, and the ingenious exercises of Cheng Zhong, were the most well-received by the audience for their neatness, beauty, skill, and liveliness. In addition, the fitness dance of Wu Ben, the Scottish folk dance of Tang Wan, and the martial arts of Jing Ye were also commendable.

Track and Field Results

Yesterday, a total of nine events, including performance groups, were held as finals. Among them, Wang Yechao from Yangjing District broke the record of 11.79 meters held by Zhang Zhaotong of Guang Gong, with a throw of 12.625 meters in the boys' Group C shot put, which was most commendable. In the preliminary rounds, the results in the boys' Group B 200-meter race were the best. Ju Weiren of Fa Hua ran 28.1 seconds, and Chen Guoyao of Te Yi ran 28.4 seconds, both breaking the record of 28.8 seconds held by Zhang Yanqing of Guang Gong. Zhao Zhongfang of Yangjing equaled the record. The results in the other events were also quite good.

Finals Sketches

In the boys' Group A 800-meter race, there were as many as thirty-seven participants. After two laps around the field, more than ten people dropped out midway. Jin Zhaosheng led all the way and reached the finish line in 2 minutes and 24.8 seconds. With effort, it would not be difficult to break the record, which was about five seconds faster. Shan Miaoquan had enough energy at the beginning, but near the finish line, he gradually became discouraged, finishing only twenty meters behind Jin Zhaosheng in second place.

Luo Shouxuan won the boys' Group A long jump with a jump of 5.14 meters. His posture was quite good, and he is indeed a promising talent. Wu Chunhua was second with 4.93 meters, Jin Guangyao was third with 4.69 meters, Dai Xingliang was fourth with 4.64 meters, Yao Shungeng was fifth with 4.56 meters, and Lei Rong was sixth with 4.515 meters.

Wang Yechao made great progress compared to his performance in the preliminary selection, breaking the record yesterday with a throw of 12.625 meters in the boys' Group C shot put. Li Baochang was also not weak with a throw of 11.20 meters. Zhang Ming was third with 11.19 meters, Gai Xiangyin was fourth with 10.20 meters, Zhong Zichao was fifth with 10.19 meters, and Xu Songlin was sixth with 10 meters.

Wu Fanglin's posture in the boys' Group B high jump lacked training, so after clearing 1.335 meters, he still had leg strength but could not clear the bar. Second to fourth place were all 1.27 meters, and fifth place was 1.21 meters.

The girls' Group C standing long jump had the most participants. Chen Yonghua jumped 2.02 meters, second place jumped 1.95 meters, third place jumped 1.93 meters, fourth place jumped 1.92 meters, fifth place jumped 1.90 meters, and sixth place jumped 1.89 meters. The differences were very small.

Odds and Ends from the Venue

Yesterday was the first day of the eighth annual Shanghai Elementary School Joint Sports Meet. Of all the events, the grand drill performance by three thousand elementary school students was undoubtedly the most eye-catching and spectacular scene. On a vast, verdant lawn, three thousand children in white uniforms were arranged in a highly disciplined manner in the center. From a distance, it looked like a large carpet woven with patterns, truly beautiful. When they finished each movement, applause erupted from all sides. Finally, under the leadership of the commander, the children shouted "Long Live the Republic of China" three times, their loud slogans touching the hearts of the adults. Patriotic enthusiasm instantly permeated the entire venue, leaving a deep impression on everyone.

Yesterday was the third day of mourning for Mr. Hu Hanmin, a founding father of our Party and nation. The national flag, party flag, and the event's flag at the venue were all flown at half-mast. Their fluttering in the alternately rainy and overcast sky added immeasurable sorrow to the festive event.

This was the first time that the elementary school sports meet was held at the Municipal Stadium. The number of students who attended yesterday was not small, totaling over seven or eight thousand. If it had been held at the Dajilu Stadium, it would have been overcrowded long ago. But here, except for the area around the west command platform, which was crowded with people, the north and south stands were quite deserted. This shows the capacity of this massive structure.

The various school gymnastics performances yesterday totaled more than fifty. One after another, they exhausted all kinds of ingenuity. It was like being on a road in Shanyin, with so much to see that one could barely keep up. In terms of the performance results, they were generally good. Perhaps they had undergone a long period of preparation beforehand. Naturally, the poor ones would not show their faces here.

Passing the weight check is something that athletes generally dread. Often, a slight difference can lead to the cancellation of their earned points. To ensure that they did not exceed the prescribed weight, some starved themselves beforehand, while others took off their clothes and washed their feet during the weigh-in. The situation was quite miserable.

Performances by kindergarten students have long been recognized as interesting events. However, yesterday there were only a few items such as Cheng Dong's "Baby Soldiers," Shanghai's "Little Army," and Qi Mei's "Little Swallows." Moreover, the costumes were more casual than in previous years. This may also be due to the impact of the economic downturn.

The championship system in this session takes districts as the unit, breaking the old habit of competition between schools. According to the current situation, Hu Nan and Te Yi districts are the most promising winners of the championship. He An Elementary School is the head of the Te Yi district. There were a particularly large number of cheering students from that school, perched on the side of the command platform, with extraordinary enthusiasm. Whenever they saw a student from their district win, they waved flags and shouted, their voices shaking the stands. The children's enthusiasm was unconsciously revealed.
