Special Education Conference of Five Provinces: Decides That Each Education Department of the Five Provinces Will Set Up a Special Education Section 156

(Nanjing, 14th) The Special Education Conference of the Five Provinces held a discussion meeting at 9:00 AM on the 14th. Twenty-seven people attended, including Minister Wang, Wei Changweng Wenhào, He Zhonghan, Chen Jianxiu, Duan Xipeng, and the heads of the education departments of the five provinces. Minister Wang presided over the meeting and delivered a speech, stating that the Ministry of Education will continue to handle special education in the five provinces and should strive for methods that are in line with economic conditions. The heads of the education departments of the five provinces then gave reports. The chairman then appointed committees for reviewing proposals in each group. The first group was convened by Yang Lian, the second group by Chen Jianxiu, and the third group by Lei Zhen, who held group meetings separately. All reviews were completed by noon. The discussion meeting resumed at 2:30 PM in the afternoon, chaired by Chairman Wang, who first reported on the results of the review and then discussed the proposals, all of which were decided separately. The meeting ended at 5:00 PM. It is reported that the most important outcome of the discussions regarding administration was the decision that each education department of the five provinces will set up a special education section dedicated to handling special education matters. Existing capable inspectors will be retained in their positions. Regarding the ratio of expenditure, it was decided that project funds would account for 88% to 95%, and reserve funds would account for 5% to 12%. Regarding the curriculum, the standards for the amount of curriculum will be left to the standing committee for discussion.

Regarding the various rules and regulations for review and judging, although they have been drafted separately by the judging committee and approved by the preparatory committee, they should be reviewed again for caution. The decision was to amend and pass them. Municipal Council Actively Preparing: Citywide Boy Scout Conference; Mayor Wu and Others Serve as Chairman and Vice-Chairman; Set to Open in the City Center on the 5th of Next Month; Group Course Competition Items Have Been Specified; Group Leader Discussion Set for the 18th of This Month 158

The Boy Scout movement in this city has been under the leadership of the Party and government since 1928 and has held a citywide Boy Scout review and encampment once a year to assess past training achievements and learn lessons for future training. The first one was held in 1929, with only a few hundred Boy Scouts participating. Since then, the number of participants has increased year by year, reaching over five thousand at the sixth event last year. This year's event will continue as usual, and it is estimated that more than ten thousand people will participate. The Municipal Boy Scout Council is actively preparing for it. Details are as follows:

Changing the Name; Specifying the Plan

The citywide Boy Scout gathering has been referred to as the "Grand Review and Encampment" in previous years. The scope seemed narrow, so starting this year, it will be renamed the "Grand Conference," which has a broader meaning and can encompass all Boy Scout activities. The date of the seventh Grand Conference has been set from June 5th to 9th, totaling five days. Wu Tiecheng, Tong Xingbai, and Pan Gongzhan have been hired to serve as chairman and vice-chairman. The location will be in the city center, with the camping area in the square in front of the Municipal Government. The review and course competitions, campfire and other activities will be held at the Municipal Stadium. The funds will be allocated from the municipal treasury. In addition to the review, camping, and course competitions, this conference will add labor service and emergency period Boy Scout mobilization exercises. Many experts in Boy Scout affairs have been hired to undertake design and guidance.

Course Competitions: Organized by Group

This course competition will be organized into five groups: middle school Boy Scouts, middle school Girl Scouts, elementary school Boy Scouts, elementary school Girl Scouts, and social Boy Scouts. The middle school Boy Scout group items include: First Aid, Surveying, Drafting, English Semaphore, English Single Flag, Stroke Semaphore, Bridge Building, Observation Tower, Night Navigation, and other nine types. The middle school Girl Scout group items include: Knot Tying, Observation, First Aid, English Semaphore, English Single Flag, Stroke Semaphore, Sewing, Cooking, Singing, and other nine types. The elementary school Boy Scout group items include: Discipline, Knot Tying, Singing, Morse Code Semaphore, Observation, First Aid, and other six types. The elementary school Girl Scout group items include: Discipline, Singing, Morse Code Semaphore, First Aid, Sewing, and other six types. The social Boy Scout group items are the same as the middle school Boy Scout group.

Convening Group Leaders: Reporting Methods

It is also reported that there are restrictions on participation. Each middle school and social group is limited to participating in four items, and each elementary school group is limited to participating in three items. Scores will not be counted if fewer participate. Each Boy Scout can participate in at most two competitions. All methods for the conference have been drafted and approved by the Municipal Boy Scout Council and will be issued to each group soon. It is understood that the council has scheduled a discussion meeting for all group leaders on Monday, the 18th of this month, at 4:30 PM at the YMCA on Sichuan Road to report on all methods to facilitate progress. The school board will be responsible for handling the conclusion.

Ministry of Education Order: Suzhou Zhongshan Physical Education Academy to Cease Operations; Board of Directors to Handle Closure 159

(Zhenjiang Correspondence) The private Suzhou Zhongshan Physical Education Academy, since the resignation of the Chairman of the Board of Directors, Jia Shiyi, and the departure of the Principal, Zhu Chongming, to Japan, has been without responsible leadership. The Ministry of Education previously issued an order to the Department of Education, urging them to swiftly instruct the academy's board of directors to convene a meeting to resolve all issues, and stipulating that no enrollment could occur without Ministry approval until a sound reorganization plan was in place. Subsequently, the Ministry dispatched personnel for inspection. It was reported that the board of directors had convened only once, without any records, and that management was poor. An order has been issued to immediately cease operations, with the board of directors responsible for handling the closure. All student records will be invalidated. The Ministry has already instructed the relevant authorities to direct the academy to comply and report accordingly.

The price of No. 120 "Sky Bridge" brand private goods remained unchanged at over 300 yuan. Transactions remained sluggish. Although no private goods have been transported in recently, 2800 *pi* of private goods woven products, such as Minghua Ge and thread-woven fabrics, were shipped from North China yesterday. Although they were once detained by the North Railway Station, they were immediately released. The selling price of these goods is low, making it difficult for local silk factories to compete, so the market prospects are not optimistic. Yesterday, local silk factories purchased several boxes of No. 120 "Seeking Profit Factory" brand "Sun" bright silk at 265 yuan, several boxes of No. 100 "Flying Lion" brand dull silk at 400 yuan, and several boxes of No. 100 "Three Tree" brand dull silk at 380 yuan.

North-South Goods: High-Quality Preserved Mustard Greens Remain Deadlocked 178

Sichuan preserved mustard greens have been scarce recently due to limited arrivals, with high-end varieties particularly in short supply. The supply is limited. Top-grade Leqi preserved mustard greens from the upper village are in demand in the Nanyang area. Merchants are demanding higher prices, showing signs of trying to buy low and sell high. However, the base price is already high, and merchants are mostly buying and selling on the go, not daring to speculate. Yesterday, the Juyutong trading house quoted 27 yuan for top-grade Leqi preserved mustard greens, but no deal was made, showing a stalemate. Market prices for Leqi preserved mustard greens were 26-27 yuan for top-grade, 23-24 yuan for ordinary, 24-25 yuan for top-grade Peiling preserved mustard greens, and 22-23 yuan for the next grade. The price of top-grade Fengdu preserved mustard greens was similar, with subsequent grades reduced accordingly, up by 1.5 yuan compared to the first ten days of the month.

Damage to Lychee Flower Seedlings in Haikou 179

Haikou lychee this spring's flower seedlings were quite lush, raising hopes for a bumper harvest. However, recent wind and rain damage, coupled with insect infestations, have caused significant losses. It is predicted that this year's harvest will only be about 50-60% of the potential.

Seafood: Dried Fish Maw and Bird's Nest Soar, Dried Scallops Stagnant and Decline 180

The current supply of dried scallops is limited, and inventories are also low. The market originally hoped for an increase in prices. Unfortunately, sales are extremely sluggish, and there is little interest in new arrivals, causing prices to trend downwards. Yesterday, merchants in the market were selling medium-sized, fresh-colored, good-quality Northern scallops at 164 yuan, those with less vibrant color at 160 yuan, extra-large ones at 157-158 yuan, triangular ones at 160 yuan, and broken pieces at 156 yuan. Few merchants were willing to purchase.

Both dried fish maw supplies and inventories are scarce, failing to meet demand. The market is very brisk. Yesterday, it was heard that top-quality goods were offered at 375 yuan per case, and second-quality goods at 330 yuan per two-case, an increase of 20-30 yuan per *dang* compared to the previous transactions. Merchants are in great need of goods, and everyone is vying to buy them, thus driving the price up so significantly.

Domestic bird's nest from Ningbo, Wenzhou, and Yantai, etc., are currently out of stock. Both coarse and fine varieties of Japanese bird's nest have also been out of stock for a long time. Only medium-sized strips are available on the market, selling for 58 yuan. Inferior, yellow, broken-belly goods are also selling for 48 yuan. The market has reached its peak. Being at a high position is dangerous, and if more goods arrive, the market is expected to fall back down.

Metals: Antimony Continues to Fall 181

Last weekend, antimony was quoted at 750 yuan per ton, but transactions were few. Recently, factories have been releasing their inventories, and fellow traders have also been selling on the market, causing prices to drop sharply. The price has fallen to 735 yuan per ton, but there are still no buyers. Fellow traders with tight funds are eager to sell at even lower prices (willing to sell at 730 yuan per ton), but due to the unfavorable environment, there are few buyers. Apart from a small amount of trading, there are no major transactions to report. It is said that yesterday, only 20-30 *dan* were traded by the Hongkou gang.

Shen Bao Literary and Art Weekly

Reunion 182

— Yingzi

—Reminiscence of Bailing Temple—

Spring in the frontier regions seems to arrive particularly late. It's already late spring in March. In Jiangnan, it's said to be the time of birds flying in flocks, right? But the frontier regions have been constantly experiencing spring snow, one after another. Although spring snow isn't as cold as winter snow and melts as soon as it lands, the snow on the Daqing Mountains freezes as soon as it falls, making the climate icy cold.

However, spring finally arrived in the frontier regions. During Qingming Festival, a great yellow wind blew for a whole day, with flying sand and rocks striking people's faces. In the evening, it even started raining, with raindrops falling like scattered beans! Cold and hard. The weather was like that of late autumn, chilling people to the bone, making them shiver. I staggered down the street, wrapped in a woolen blanket, wanting to go home. Inadvertently, I met a group of people. The person in front, carrying a cane, wearing an indigo blue cotton gown, a middle-aged man with red pockmarks on his face, nodded. I also nodded subconsciously. Suddenly, I couldn't remember who this person being polite to me was. Later, I realized that it was that Iron Faction guy, the one who tormented my good friend when he went to Bailing last year? People are such forgetful creatures. If it weren't for his back shrouded in an "indigo blue" gown and that special countenance with pockmarks, I really wouldn't have remembered who he was.

Remembering that it was him, I couldn't help but be gripped by the anger of the past. This guy who prevented me from seeing the Mongolian scenery of Bailing Temple, he's running here again. Isn't he congratulating himself in that treasure country created by one of the Allied nations?

Past events were peeled out layer by layer like a cocoon. It hasn't even been a year since I left Bailing Temple. How could I not remember how I felt at this time a year ago, enduring humiliation alone in the Mongolian yurt in Bailing Temple, suffering torment in the Mongolian wilderness?

When I went to Bailing Temple, it was precisely when the × Association and the × Provincial Government were in an irreconcilable dispute over tax revenue. Because of the animosity between the two sides, the frontier newspaper, as the official newspaper of the × Government, greatly attacked and mocked the × Association. As a small employee in the frontier news industry, I certainly knew that going to the central area of the × Association, Bailing Temple, at this time would be like courting misfortune. However, due to a long-held desire to see the Mongolian scenery and the fact that I was accompanying over sixty boys and girls, I pretended to be one of the boys and girls and took the risk. I didn't expect to be recognized halfway, and the one who recognized me was this gentleman who nodded to me today!

After passing through the Daqing Mountains, due to waiting for two broken-down cars in the isolated city of "Wuchuan," I stayed there. I was exposed by a local acquaintance who I had met but wasn't familiar with. The next day, as soon as I left Wuchuan City, this × Association section chief with a face full of red pockmarks saw me getting on the bus and inquired about me from the temporary leader of the boys and girls. The car kept driving north, passing through the endless prairie. Ahead was still the boundless Mongolian wilderness. At this time, this gentleman with red pockmarks asked me to get out of the car. I looked around. The wilderness was a haze of gray, and the wind was howling on the prairie. Needless to say, there wasn't a single sign of human life within a hundred miles, not even a single cow or sheep. My burning desire for survival made me refuse to get out of the car. Then, the section chief suggested to me: "In order to prevent the person in charge from being unfavorable to you when we arrive at Bailing Temple, I won't let you stay in the Mongolian yurt or civilian houses." That was also to express that he was afraid I would suffer hardships.

When we arrived at Bailing Temple, after crossing the small river, the car stopped in front of the Mongolian yurt. The section chief asked me to do what he had told me to do halfway. In the twilight, I widened my eyes and looked around again. Besides the scattered sixty or seventy Mongolian yurts, to the west was Bailing Temple shining in the evening glow, to the east of the river were some mud houses, and besides that, there was only the half-bald mountain behind the Mongolian yurt, the vast wilderness, and I was like a baby being abandoned on it. Blown by the wind, hit by the sand, and maybe even buried in the belly of a beast if a wild animal came out at night. My desire for survival was never stronger than at this moment. I insisted that the section chief find me a place to stay. I knew that besides the Mongolian yurts, the temple, and the houses east of the river, where else could I stay?

Fortunately, this red-pockmarked section chief still didn't have the determination to kill me. I finally entered the Mongolian yurt under the urgent requests of some of the boys and girls. However, conditions came with it: "Until the time you leave Bailing Temple, you are not allowed to leave the yurt."

The next day, after being awakened by the sound of the bugle, I looked at the green sky on the dome of the Mongolian yurt from the cold bedding spread on the ground, feeling troubled: "Should I go out or not?" I hesitated. Finally, because there was no place for me to relieve myself in the Mongolian yurt, I boldly went out.

Ah! What good would it do to go out!

After looking at the "Obo" on the back of the mountain behind the Mongolian yurt and the vast prairie in front, the boys and girls all went to visit the temple. Only I was restricted by people and had to stay in the yurt dumbly. "Don't go to see the temple, if you go, you'll be arrested!" In the yurt, I felt lonely, angry, and afraid, tormented by these words that hurt my young heart. What do other people's petty matters have to do with me? However, however!……

In this way, I spent half a day in the Mongolian yurt, reading to pass the time that felt especially long. Now, looking back, reading in the Mongolian yurt is probably an opportunity that I will never have again.

Except for being forced by loneliness to bravely take a look at the east of the river, I only mixed with the boys and girls in the evening to listen to a burst of Mongolian music and singing, and I also went with the boys and girls to see the yurt of a certain prince where the statue of "Genghis Khan" was enshrined. Besides that, I couldn't even see the Mongolians riding horses.

Until the morning of the third day when I left Bailing Temple, this red-pockmarked section chief was still explaining to me. Even at this time, he was still explaining to me. I really didn't know what his psychology was at that time.

Sitting in the original car again and leaving Bailing Temple, looking at the yellow flags waving in front of the Mongolian yurt, my eyes were filled with tears. I wasn't sad about the grievances I had suffered. I was going back with a heart full of regret. I was thinking about whether I would have the chance to come to Bailing Temple again to see the Mongolian scenery! Would the cruel reality allow me to come again?

Ah!

In this bleak and rainy season, I actually reunited with this red-pockmarked section chief. In this cold rain, my heart burned even more like it was doused with oil. The scene of Bailing Temple appeared before my eyes again.

I once said: "Why should one feel regret for not seeing Bailing Temple, which is often seen like the Guihua Sheritu Zhao Temple!" Now, I deny my words. That is Mongolian scenery! Moreover, in today's world, will people still allow me to go to Bailing Temple to see it?

But suddenly, I thought about this red-pockmarked section chief who was enjoying happiness in the kingdom under the kingly way paradise, and now he actually ran to this place. Thinking about the day when this place would also become a "kingly way paradise," my heart couldn't help but shiver in the cold rain.

Exodus 183

— Xicen

Walking, watching groups of people leave this ancient mountain city. In a blink of an eye, it's already October.

Getting up early in the morning, I often go up to the city walls. Gradually, I can see the mountain colors all around. In some places, they have long turned from distant green shadows to solid dark blue. This is a sign of autumn. It seems that wherever autumn's footsteps tread, the colors fade. In fact, it's just that the leaves on the mountain trees have fallen off. In a few more days, I'm afraid this dark blue will reveal the scorched red or yellow again.

"Depart, depart..."

Hearing such orders, issued from my own fingers. Every time I finish such work, I can't help but lean back in my rattan chair and think. Yes, once: the day we leave is really getting closer. In the past few days, several overly nervous companions have been packing up their odds and ends. Immediately, this courtyard is filled with chaos everywhere, which carries with it the desolation of all departures.

I have lived in this mountain city for almost two years. Although there is gray everywhere here, people are just wrapped in gray, living a hard and bleak life. Collapse, bankruptcy, even in the mountains, people often talk about recent decline. I dare not imagine; what color is on the faces of people who eat rotten vegetable leaves or bark as food. Therefore, every time I hear about the methods of harassment by the ×× in the countryside, such as beatings, extortion, ... I am always very angry. Piglets, piglets, it's really not a human life! It's too gray here, and I sometimes yearn for the distance.

The date of the real departure is before my eyes, and I can't help but feel reluctant to part. Last night, I even saw two companions running up the city walls to wind around, looking at the distant mountains, very disheartened.

Last night, it revealed the taste of the eve of departure. At first, as soon as it got dark, I still wanted to go talk to them. But I pulled open every screen door, and there wasn't a single figure inside.

"The ghosts have grabbed them..."

As a result, I fell into a drowsy sleep out of loneliness. Later, I remembered that they must have each gone to their respective mistresses. From this, I connected to this mountainous area that I had clearly understood in the past two years. It's simply a piece of soil with not a bit of stickiness in the middle, resulting in poverty everywhere. This is just a simple mountain town. Although I don't know how far the city walls are, walking around the entire circle every evening, calculating it, wouldn't take more than half an hour. Yet even this simple little place is full of darkness. Thinking of the cruelty of those who exploit the flesh, I can't help but think of the pity of selling my soul.

Being dissolved by a kind of poison here, under the oppression of the ××, people have no freedom to breathe loudly.

Once, a very extraordinary event occurred. A junior officer in the team went missing. As a result, a day later, his body was found abandoned in a grove of trees outside the south gate after being murdered. Above, there were villagers in the mountains... He squeezed out. Of course, there was also a bit of romance interspersed in the middle, but I would say it was more like crude lust. But this confession has been hidden all along. Now that we are about to leave, I suppose only we ourselves know about it, apart from the murderer.

A night of dissipation is naturally easy to get through. As soon as dawn breaks, we will have arrived at the day of departure.

Behind my house to the north is a large forest. I vaguely heard it in my dream. There was the sound of bells of... very relaxed; ringing once, ringing once. There were also footsteps coming and going. But that was even lower and softer. You couldn't hear it clearly unless you held your breath.

White light permeated the window paper. People outside started bustling about, and the sound of talking quickly passed by, as if everyone was busy walking.

Regarding departure, I didn't bear any responsibility except for the obligation to obey, sit on the... and leave this place. So, whether I got up early or late didn't matter much. But looking at the empty house with only one or two rickety chairs left, I didn't want to sleep anymore. So I got up and watched my followers fasten my luggage, bedding, and quilt to the designated... Immediately, the mood of waiting for departure was quickly submerged by the early cold in the mountains. Looking at the chrysanthemums planted in the center of the courtyard, all... I felt very sad. So I quietly walked out the door with two companions who were cheerful and had no tasks.

It was extremely deserted in front of the gate. No soldiers were shouting "Salute" at you anymore. Only a group of children stood across the street, their eyes wide with surprise.

We walked down the street in the early wind, wrapped in coats. Finally, we arrived at the small tavern where we often went to drink.

"One last time, buddy..."

The three of us had this feeling. We looked at each other, but no one said anything. The waiter in the shop probably had anticipated our visit so early today. He smiled without hesitation and greeted us.

I knew that only today's smile was genuine, and it wasn't directed at us, but at the news of our departure today. Although they usually earn our money, ×× is contradictory: the lower they are, the more they will rely on gray clothes to do unreasonable things. Therefore, although they welcome the money we send on the one hand, they can't help but curse those more numerous brothers on the other hand.

People who have drunk alcohol don't feel cold, so we didn't go back and instead went straight out of the south gate to wait for them to go.

Standing on the stone bridge, looking at the shadows of temples on the surrounding mountain peaks, I felt a sense of awe. It was still when the peach blossoms were blooming in March. On a holiday, many of our companions had taken a trip there. I remember lying under the peach trees before sunset, looking at the downhill roads interspersed among the chaotic mountains, and imagining home. Now we are really leaving, going down the mountain. It was a foggy day when we came two years ago. Today, there should be rustling leaves on the clear autumn mountain rocks.

Part of the... team had already walked past. The sun also reddened half of the mountain, and kept reddening the stream under the bridge, choking low.

Finally, they came. My companions were all laughing and talking about how the people in the city lit firecrackers to send us off. I turned my head to look at the city walls, but they stood there silently, without any familiar traces. Sitting on the..., swaying with the sound of the bells, going up the mountain, I was still thinking about the sound of firecrackers in people's hands!

Anniversary 184

— Fang Yin

In an instant, a whole year has passed,

But your tomb is still the same as last autumn—

Let the fierce west wind blow mercilessly,

Let the crippled white bones be buried coldly.

The bloody wind swept across the wilderness,

Countless corpses are buried on the ridges,

Whether they were enemies or friends in life,

Now they are arranged the same way as you.

The sound of insects accompanies you through the eternal autumn nights,

Every year, the white snow fills the desolate tombs.

Who dares to say that the spring breeze can blow away the wild fire,

Will tomorrow not ignite the entire wilderness?

Bovarism 185

— Zhiying

The term "Bovarism" was coined by Jules de Gaultier. He wrote a lengthy novel dedicated to Gustave Flaubert's "Madame Bovary," extensively discussing personal Bovarism and collective Bovarism. As one of the psychological manifestations of art and literature, it is highly meaningful and refreshing to examine it to some extent.

Although Flaubert's "Madame Bovary" has long been translated into Chinese, it has not received widespread attention. In France, however, it is a monumental work in literary history. Flaubert himself said, "My poor Madame Bovary must be suffering and weeping in many villages in France." This is not an exaggeration. Madame Bovary is a unique character who also represents universal human psychology. In this work, romanticism and realism are intertwined. Rich imagination and realistic depiction give it an immortal artistic brilliance. This is what we should know before examining Bovarism.

So, what is Bovarism?

Gaultier believed it to be "the power of man to conceive himself as other than he is" (Le pouvoir departia Phomme de se concevoir autre qu'il n-'eit).

This is a psychological function of humanity at a specific historical stage. Such individuals, though possessing their own talents, sensations, and thoughts, always misunderstand their talents, misuse their sensations, and misapply their thoughts. They transform themselves and the people and things around them, resulting in comedic, tragic, and outcomes that are neither comedic nor tragic.

Let us dissect two or three of the main characters in "Madame Bovary."

Doctor Homais is a philistine bourgeois. He poses as a scientist, spouting scholarly terms, talking about everything from ancient times to the present, from east to west, south to north. He has his own prejudices, and the content of his conversations is regardless of whether others understand it or not. He has a high degree of vanity, seeing his knowledge, as insignificant as eye mucus, as great as Mount Tai. He believes in the aesthetics of realism, but due to his aristocratic tastes, he also detests the vulgarity of reality. He cannot correctly recognize what he is, just as he cannot correctly recognize external things. However, in the vulgar bourgeoisie of 1850s France, such characters were valued by the authorities and supported by public opinion. This is a caricature of the petty bourgeoisie, and Flaubert satirically portrays him as a typical vulgar bourgeois. Doctor Homais' "Bovarism" achieves a comedic outcome.

Furthermore, Rodolphe Boulanger is a typical representative of the "Bovarism" of the common bourgeois intellectuals. He has imagination but lacks the ability to act. His imagination either uses force to pull the object down to his own level or uses willpower to pull himself up to the position of the object. He lives every day in tomorrow. He feels anxious in his powerlessness and places his hope in powerlessness. He misunderstands his own sensibility and his own intelligence. He thinks he understands art very well and always wants to be a poet, novelist, and critic. Sometimes he pretends to be a philosopher, sometimes he pretends to be a historian, and sometimes he transforms into a politician. He is an ordinary vulgar person without comedic or tragic life behaviors, what Flaubert calls "dried fruit" (Fruite secs).

Madame Bovary is the most concentrated expression of "Bovarism." She is the wife of a country doctor, harboring romantic dreams, yet completely incapable. Her understanding of herself is completely wrong. She often fantasizes that she is the protagonist in a romance novel, but in reality, she is entangled in that ordinary reality. Due to the error in her self-awareness, she inevitably must distort external things.

"Her life is a succession of all illusions. First, an illusion about herself, then an illusion about others, followed by an illusion about places, and an illusion about time. These illusions, when viewed in detail, are all inevitable products of her illusions about herself. That is, the inevitable product of Bovarism."

This passage is an excellent annotation of Bovarism.

When we look at Madame Bovary's entire life, it is indeed a tragicomedy of illusions. She is dissatisfied with her ordinary husband, mistakes her ideal lover, indulges in religious ecstasy, and falls into carnal pleasures. But all of this gives her the suffering of disillusionment. The closer things get to her, the more her thoughts deviate from them. In such a continuous stream of illusions, she gradually consumes her life and finally embarks on the inevitable path of tragedy.

Some commentators believe that Bovarism like this is "a function that exists in all ages and environments among human beings." This conclusion still needs to be considered. Of course, we can say that Bovarism and the spirit of Ah Q in China have some similarities; however, due to the different environments, these two things are separated by significant differences. Even in the overall view, they are almost entirely different things. The similarity between them is that they both live in a world of "fantasy," however, Ah Q's "ideal" is the ideal of a slave; Madame Bovary's "ideal" is the ideal of a petty bourgeois.

Flaubert himself said, "Madame Bovary is me." This is not a joke. Flaubert extremely loathed the life of bourgeois society. In such a society, everything is ordinary, vulgar, greedy, and selfish. People are dragged down a despicable path by an invisible thread of money, and people are like puppets of money, everything develops "involuntarily." Although Flaubert said, "I did not infuse my feelings and life into this novel at all," this is incorrect. He himself contradicted himself, saying: "The artist in his work is just like God in creation. Although the eye cannot see, it cannot be without omnipotent power. His existence can be felt everywhere, but his form must not appear." Therefore, we have confidence to believe that Madame Bovary's soul is permeated with Flaubert's spirit. He uses this to judge his era's society and judge himself.

It is said that when Cervantes was on his deathbed, someone asked him who was written in "Don Quixote," and he replied, "It is me." This and Flaubert's statement "Madame Bovary is me" are of the same model. Flaubert's fondness for Cervantes, the reason for that should probably be sought in this principle. Isn't Don Quixote also disgusted with the vulgar world and filled with romantic passion and ideals? How similar is this to Madame Bovary!

Thus, we line up Don Quixote, Ah Q, and Madame Bovary, which is quite interesting. They are three "great" characters from different historical stages! There is a thread connecting them. But should such things really exist in "all ages and environments"? If we believe that history is made by mankind, then I can briefly answer: Absolutely not!

Song and Shooting 186

— Maxim Gorky

The midday sun in July burned fiercely in the brass-colored sky. The small town was dazed in the steamy heat, occasionally disturbed by vague and messy noises, but immediately fell silent and was buried in silence. A kind of affected, nasal voice mournfully dragged out this song:

(Across the silvery river,

Across the golden desert,

I am searching for a——

Young woman's trail…)

Another deep voice harshly asked:

"What did you do this morning?"

"I did some shooting."

"How many?"

"Three."

"Did they grumble?"

"Why would they grumble?"

"You mean they didn't make a sound?"

"They didn't make a sound at all. They're all stubborn and straightforward as usual… They're all trained, you know, and they believe that even if they suffer one day—the bill must be settled sooner or later."

"Are they important people?"

"No—at least I don't think so. They were messing around in those lousy places, so I guess they weren't important people."

There was silence for a while, and then the affected voice continued to sing mournfully:

(The bright moon,

Is my guide…)

"Did you shoot too?"

"Why wouldn't I?"

(Tell me,

Where she's hiding…)

The deep voice sneered:

"You, still singing about 'young women,' you still have to mend your own shirts, just like… you bastard!"

"Wait, the young woman will come in time. Everything will come…"

(Gentle wind,

Tell me,

What are her daydreams…)

Fang Cai, translator

Returning from Singapore 187

— Li Sanlang

Thrown into the dark and stuffy cabin, I looked back at the tall skyscrapers, the swaying coconut trees, as if they were seeing off a deported vagrant.

No friends saw me off, only the man with the gun escorted me onto the ship. Thus, I left Singapore.

After a seven-day voyage, I hid dizzily in the cabin, wanting to vomit and desperately thirsty, like someone who had been ill. I heard the mate's abuse, but I pretended not to hear it, and I dreamily thought of my motherland, how had that poor motherland evolved!

However, I was very afraid that if I contracted that detestable disease, I would be thrown into the boundless waves like a dead man, forcing me to suppress my pain at all times, not moaning like those young masters or mistresses—I want to see my motherland again!

One morning, on the motherland's sea surface, I could see the distant mountain peaks, gradually revealing the tiny foreign houses. Mountains, beaches, green outlines appeared in the morning glow beneath the green sea and the azure sky.

"But that's not the motherland yet, it's Hong Kong that has blocked our country's gateway!"

However, I love the verdant mountain peaks, and the beautiful shadows reappeared in my eyes. As the ship slowly sailed into the port, the clouds and mist raced across the green peaks. Two high mountains stood opposite each other in the narrow harbor, and the beautiful houses were neatly arranged, stacked high, one level after another, all the way to the unscattered snowy sky. -- Is this a city moved from Europe to China? Isn't the smoking beach filled with large and small steamships? Perhaps even more bustling than Shanghai! It's full of coolies, moving like hungry cats. The rows of skyscrapers of large banks, restaurants, and department stores are even more prosperous than Singapore.

I took a deep breath. What I saw was almost the same as in the southern islands, but there were no dense green trees, but eyes that were even more fierce than cats chasing mice, fixed on this body that had lost its freedom.

When the ship was about to reach the dock, an Indian devil who had been escorted from Singapore to Hong Kong handed me over to the inspectors here.

"I'm handing him over to you."

The fat, pig-like Chinese man pursed his long mouth, talking to the Englishman while scanning me from head to toe, looking at the official document, which wrote down my crimes! … They stared at me with cat-like eyes, searched my body, I didn't make a sound, gritting my teeth and glaring at the insignias on their collars.

All those actions made my heart beat faster and my chest boil. I wished I could burn away their leering faces.

Only when a small electric boat came to pick me up was I taken to a steamer going inland.

My unfree body hid in a dark corner again, quietly waiting for the treatment that my motherland would give me.

Supplement to the Shanghai News

Talks

The Guangzhou Clothing Problem 188

— Xian

Since the establishment of the National Government, the clothing system has still followed the old system of the Qing Dynasty. No reforms have been made to correct the foundation. In today's country, with force as the prerequisite, the reform of clothing is especially necessary. One is to display the color of civilization, and the other is to display the spirit of martial valor. In this world of the survival of the fittest, weak countries have no room for survival. The imperialists of the world have already clearly told us.

According to recent telegrams from Guangzhou, the police have been inspecting women's clothing in theaters and entertainment venues for days, to see if they meet the standards set by the authorities. Those who violate them are taken to the police station for punishment. According to the new rules, women's clothing must be below the knee and below the elbow, and their necks must be covered. However, the long sleeves rule has been allowed to be modified due to a petition from the Guangzhou Women's Association. The Guangzhou clothing problem has been discussed in this publication before, but there has only been general opposition, and no thorough research. Since the beginning of the Republic of China, men's long robes and mandarin jackets, or suits and leather shoes, have not changed at all, while women's clothing has been constantly changing, with dazzling and strange patterns, almost changing every day. It is not impossible to impose restrictions. However, it is ridiculous that Guangzhou standard clothing must be below the knee and below the elbow, and the neck must be covered. A woman's neck is the same as a man's neck, so what is so special about it that it must be covered? This is the first strange thing. Women's short sleeves not only display the beauty of the flesh, but also the issue of showing off, and the convenience of operation is also one of the reasons. What is the meaning of opposing short sleeves? This is the second strange thing. As for clothes below the knee, it is even more difficult to understand. Now, whether men or women, clothes should be convenient and economical. If a woman is chaste, below the knee is fine, and not below the knee is also fine. If a woman is not chaste, below the knee is not fine, and not below the knee is also not fine. Isn't it that below the knee is possible to do that, and not below the knee it is not possible to do that?

However, the system of short sleeves can be strictly prohibited in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and northern places, but Guangzhou does not have to. Why is this? The climate is different. The weather in the north is cold, and women in short sleeves often get so cold that their skin turns red and purple, and even develop frostbite, which is also harmful to health. Therefore, it can be prohibited in winter, but not prohibited in spring and summer. As for Guangzhou, the weather is warm all year round, so it is meaningless to strictly prohibit it. In short. In the current era, the clothing of men and women should tend to be convenient and be able to display the spirit of martial valor. If this principle is reversed and one focuses solely on enchanting and lewd appearances, or on ancient etiquette, it is all meaningless.

As for men's clothing, it has been discussed by many people in this publication in previous years. Generally speaking, it is advocated to remove long robes and mandarin jackets and create a kind of light and simple clothing. The general opinion is that it should be a Chinese-style jacket that is only knee-length, because long robes and mandarin jackets not only completely display a weak attitude, but also have a passive atmosphere in spirit, and are also extremely inconvenient for walking. As for suits and leather shoes, although they are more stylish, wearing them is also extremely cumbersome, and the people of a country have their own clothes, so why must they learn the fur of Westerners? Now the Guangzhou authorities intend to strictly prohibit students from wearing suits, which is not impossible, but only strictly prohibiting students from wearing suits, and not strictly prohibiting other people from wearing suits, what is the reason for this? It is really puzzling.

In the Fourth-Class Cabin 189

— Menghua

In this huge ocean liner, I used fifty-six dollars to exchange for this five-foot square space. The fourth-class cabin is always without sunlight, and in this hot June weather, the sea breeze outside is howling, but there is not a trace of wind here. Next to it is the engine room, which spreads unbearable heat to these lowly fourth-class passengers. The air is like a solidified piece of aluminum, and we are even deprived of the right to breathe.

After disembarking from Singapore, my head felt like someone was constantly pricking it with needles, dizzy and painful, and I couldn't even sleep. Under the mat, however, was a black, sticky steel plate, and centipedes crawled to the edge of my mat from time to time. When I crushed them to death, their stomachs full of dirty blood made me want to vomit.

I cursed money all the time, especially when I heard the low music from above. I imagined the noble gentlemen dancing slowly on the waxed, smooth floor, singing softly, and passing the June twilight on the Indian Ocean.

But in this kind of cabin, some people are so happy. Over there, four people are playing mahjong, and nearby, five or seven people are opening a fan-tan game, and some people are playing cards. The yelling and scolding sometimes even drowned out the huge noise of the axles. They were naked, only wearing a bath towel, and on their backs, chests, and foreheads, sweat hung down like small streams, but they were concentrating, fighting against unknown gambling luck. In the hanging berth opposite, a middle-aged woman was accompanying a small oil lamp. The small red flame was covered by a pale white lampshade and looked even weaker. In this small cabin, which was no more than four square yards, deception, selfishness, obscenity, and decadent human nature overflowed along with the heat and fishy smell.

On the third day of the voyage, after checking the tickets, two more people were added to this small cabin, they were tied to an iron pillar. The woman's shirt was torn, and the man's back and legs had whip marks, and the dried bloodstains were like thick red lines, flowing down from his forehead, shoulders, chest, and calves. At first, they tried to struggle and cried miserably. After two or three hours, they were silent, burying their heads, as tired and weak as a traveler who had walked tens of thousands of miles.

"It will take half a month to get to Tangshan, and even if you steal it, you will starve to death." An old man said, "I have walked this waterway at least ten times, and no one has ever been able to steal it. Can you steal it? Alas, even your life is not worth it…" He sighed, as if immersed in terrible memories. From his words, I learned that they had secretly hidden in the cargo hold before the ship sailed. They had not slept, eaten, or drunk water, and they had secretly climbed up just on the day of the ticket inspection, so they were found.

"The captain was going to throw them into the sea, how dangerous!" The old man said and walked away.

I looked at the couple, they were like two boneless people, softly drooping their upper bodies.

Next to them, the people playing mahjong were still happy, yelling and scolding loudly, as if there were no two compatriots in distress behind them. I felt as if something powerful was pressing down on my heart, and I almost fainted.

"Uncle, you have to think of a way for them, how can they survive tonight like this? They haven't even had a drop of water."

At the cabin door, two Tangshan sailors stuck their heads in, as if searching for something. The four dim lights inside made it difficult for them to see what they were looking for, so one of them stepped into the cabin.

"Fellow villager, save them, they are almost dead." I said to those two bound people, my voice like a patient's.

The sailor waved to his companion at the cabin door, and then three people ran in, they walked over with big strides, desperately untying the big knot.

"You let them go, if the captain asks, it's none of our business." A thin-faced man said, wiping the sweat from his forehead. He was a hunchback.

"Damn you, what are you! Shameless, you are Chinese!" A sailor took a step forward, and before he could push him, he had already retreated three or four steps. He quietly retreated to that corner, trembling and sitting down, timidly watching the commotion.

In front of these two victims was a pile of white rice and pickles, and also a peeled pineapple. People looked at them with pity. The woman lowered her head, staring blankly at the rice bowl, and couldn't swallow a mouthful of rice for a long time. Her shoulders twitched violently, and tears of gratitude flowed from her deeply sunken eye sockets like broken beads.

That night, I began to close my tired eyelids, but I suddenly woke up in the middle of the night. The sound of the sea waves outside was roaring. I listened to the sound of the water until dawn, and I didn't close my eyes again.

Loquat 190

— Xia Lishi

The weather is getting hot, which reminds me that it's the season for loquats to be on the market in my hometown. This unique southern fruit is something to be nostalgic for; especially since my aunt's house has an orchard.

It was a very large vegetable garden. Every time I went to my aunt's house, my cousin would take me inside to see if any fruits were ripe. Among the pomelos, longans, lychees, and various other fruits, I liked loquats the most. And there were especially many loquat trees in that orchard. Walking in through the fence at the garden entrance, seeing the trees full of loquats, I would get very excited, tugging at my cousin's hand and shouting, "The loquats are ripe! The loquats are ripe!" incessantly. Then, I would climb the tree, my cousin would hold the basket below, and a large bunch of loquats would fill the basket. Thinking I could eat my fill, I would happily shout from the tree, making my cousin urge me from below; at the same time, she was afraid I might fall down if I wasn't careful.

Bringing the loquats into the courtyard, after dinner, with the cool breeze blowing, we, four or five people, would sit around in a circle, and start eating and talking. My aunt was a woman good at talking, and she and my mother seemed to have endless things to say, often talking until we wanted to sleep. Once, sitting beside them, I heard my aunt say that her family's situation was getting worse year by year, and since my uncle passed away, they had gradually borrowed a lot of money, and the orchard was mortgaged. Naturally, if things continued like this, one day the orchard would become someone else's; then I would no longer have the happiness of climbing the loquat trees.

There was also a time when I got sick from eating too many loquats. My aunt looked at me from afar, comforting me with a gentle expression, and also said that there were still a lot of loquats, and as long as I got well, I could go to her place. I lay in bed, responding with a grateful smile. I wanted to ask her why my cousin hadn't come, but in the end, I couldn't bring myself to say it.

As soon as I got better, I went to my aunt's house again. My mother kept telling me not to be too greedy, and I nodded in agreement. This time, I was really a little afraid of getting sick again, so I just played with my cousin in the orchard. We lingered, reluctant to leave, until dusk arrived.

During this time, I left my hometown once, which was exactly the season when the loquat trees were full of fruit. My aunt gave me a large basket, and even after eating them all the way to where I was going, there were still many left. So I took them as gifts for the people there. They also loved loquats, so they were very happy; and they listened to me tell stories about loquats. Such days passed quickly, and it was late autumn when I returned to my hometown.

A cool breeze blew on me, and the gray clouds in the sky looked very dim. I stayed at home for one night, and the next morning I went to see my aunt and cousin. When I got there, the atmosphere was a little different. Although my aunt greeted me with a smile, her face seemed to have some worries, which she couldn't hide no matter what. My cousin's expression was very melancholy, and she kept her head down, not saying a word. I asked her to go to the orchard with me; she seemed a little embarrassed, but she didn't refuse me. So, we pushed open the fence, and the afternoon sunlight shone through the gaps in the leaves onto the soil, spreading over it like patterns. The late autumn wind blew the leaves, rustling. Yellow leaves were withering, falling down; the scene in the orchard looked very sad.

Yes, later I learned that the orchard had changed hands and was no longer my aunt's. The sorrow of a declining family was something I didn't yet feel personally: I only felt that when the loquat season came the following year, there would be no more basket after basket of loquats to eat.

Everything in my hometown is unbearable to recall. What is the situation now? What I cannot forget are the abundant orchard, the ripe loquats, and the faces of my aunt's family...

Cat 191

— Hua Mu

The lights are off, and you can see the moon hanging in the corner of the sky outside the window, round and bright, like a naive girl standing far away with shy charm, secretly watching the people inside the window. On such a gentle and beautiful midnight, one should be able to sleep peacefully. Many beautiful dreams are waiting for me. Just as I thought of this, I heard the cat's meow: I know this is the white cat I often see on the wall outside the window, maybe it encountered some disappointing things somewhere and jumped to the top of the wall to lament its fate. This situation has long aroused my concern. I thought to myself that this cat must have its own unutterable misfortune; because on the roof tiles nearby, there are other cats making romantic affairs that disturb people's dreams at night, which can be distinguished from their passionate meows. But this cat doesn't seem to care much about what its kind is doing, it always drags its disappointed tail, quietly walks over, and quietly walks away, lonely patrolling the night, doing nothing to contend with the world, nothing to do with the world? This little place on the top of the wall seems to be its only resting place. Lonely cat.

, it is meowing so lonely again, it sounds like it's right at my upstairs window. I think it may know that within this wide-open upstairs window, there is me, still awake in the middle of the night, hearing its meow and caring about everything about it. I believe it has already recognized me, because I have seen it jump onto the wall from somewhere several times during the day; when it encounters me leaning against the window, it will raise its round head, open its sad eyes, and exchange a few glances with me. Its expression seems to be full of suspicion about everything, and very indifferent, it treats me the same way, without fear, and without showing any intention of asking for intimacy. It comes, squats on the top of the wall, raises its foot to wash its face, looks at the sparrows jumping and wagging their tails on the corner of the building, spacing out for a moment; sometimes a burst of cooing pigeon bells suddenly flies through the sky, or a black shadow of some bird flashes past it, and it twitches its two ears, stares blankly at the sky, at this time, its expression also becomes more lively. Its eyes will also meet my eyes that are watching it, and suddenly, it seems like we have touched a tacit understanding of friendship, , the sound is sent up so light and peaceful, and I inexplicably feel a kind of joy in my heart.

Whose cat is it? I often ask myself this question. Looking at its expression, it looks very much like an abandoned cat with no home to rely on, but even if it has a home, its owner must not treat it with much care and love. If my speculation is correct, then the things it suffers from being bullied by others in its life will be unavoidable. The cold looks between its kind, the bullying of dogs, the ruthless broom in the hands of the maid, and even the evil deeds of wild children, these unfortunate blows will become encounters that will not be lacking in daily life. Besides being exhausted from running around to deal with these headaches and spending its days, there is only a little short time left, but it is a human loneliness that cannot be expressed after thinking about it. Is the top of this small wall its resting and playing place? No! It is ultimately a frustrated cat. The distance between humans and animals is so great, even if I care about it, I can't use my words to eliminate this separation, let alone give it affection and love.

Thinking of this, I put on my clothes, and I naturally saw it, its lonely appearance more obvious in the faint moonlight. Maybe it was an unexpected joy, , it meowed so softly again, what words can I use to ask it back? This poor cat. So I thought of the talking cat in fairy tales, if it could speak human language, or if I could speak cat language, not only could I express the sympathy in my heart, comfort it, and encourage it. In this sleepless midnight, could we not pour out the private thoughts stored in our chests? Human beings also have a feeling of loneliness in life.

Tokyo Odds and Ends 192

— Lei Shiyu

(4) Dance Halls

This is a very regrettable thing. I don't know how to dance, and I haven't learned it, and I haven't even been to a dance hall for sightseeing. However, I have noticed that dance halls in Tokyo are very prosperous, especially in the bustling areas of Shinjuku, Ginza, and Asakusa, there are many magnificent dance halls. Those dance halls that specialize in the business of Chinese students seem to be doing very well. "Studying in Japan News" once published a shocking statistic that the amount of money spent by students there is about tens of thousands of yuan per month. This needless to say is a kind of consumption of the sons of bureaucrats and the playboys among the students.

When I was studying Japanese at a certain cram school, a certain gentleman in the front row of me was the best at dancing. He said that he spent almost one or two yuan every night. He was the son of a capitalist. He had "studied" in France for more than two years. Because he spent too much money, his father wanted him to transfer to Japan. Fortunately, the cost of living in Japan was not high, and dancing was much cheaper than in Shanghai. It seemed that one yuan could buy more than one and a half times the tickets in Shanghai, so he lived a very comfortable life. When he was in class, you could just call him and he could take out ten bills. But I don't know why, at that time I didn't have the slightest interest in dancing, and I couldn't even raise my head to "sightsee".

Last year, Japanese newspapers published that the authorities had issued an order strictly prohibiting students from entering dance halls and cafes, but the conditions were so favorable, only prohibiting them from entering in uniform. Poor students only have one or two sets of uniforms, but for rich students, isn't it good to wear their various beautiful Western suits?

Dance girls and cafe girls were afraid that their lives would suffer a miserable fate, so each sent representatives to negotiate with the authorities. I don't know what the result was. But soon, the doors of the cafes were posted with signs inviting students to patronize. Needless to say, the dance halls were the same, like a river. Then this official formality is a waste of energy and effort. However, this is to decorate "morality" and "etiquette". This decoration does no harm to itself, and does not cause any damage to our Chinese students. One party uses such decoration to shake the face of dignity without affecting the consumption of some of the students, and the other party's students are still not prevented from seeking entertainment, isn't that getting the best of both worlds?

"Avatar Girl" Blushes and Turns Red 193

— Bai Mu

Skinny Monkey Han Langen plays a very gluttonous and timid idiot in the upcoming Yi Hua new film "Avatar Girl". One day, because he wanted to buy some cosmetics to win the favor of his beloved girlfriend, he gritted his teeth and asked his father for four mao. However, his father was very serious, and as a result, he got a scolding instead. He backed out and wandered in the yard for a long time, and then he changed his mind and walked to his cousin Yuan Meiyun's room. At this time, Yuan Meiyun was leaning on the sofa reading a book called "Women's Physiology and Hygiene". Seeing him walking in in a panic, she couldn't help but blush and turn red, and her embarrassment was more pitiful than the state of Skinny Monkey being condemned in front of his father. However, Skinny Monkey did not pay attention to the book Yuan Meiyun was reading. At first, he was like a flirting daughter, embarrassed for a long time, and finally spent a lot of effort to ask her for money. Yuan Meiyun hesitated and asked him how much he wanted, and he bent four fingers to mean borrowing four mao, but Yuan Meiyun lent him four yuan. This time, Skinny Monkey was overjoyed. So, in a little while, he had already bought a lot of cosmetics such as snow cream and white powder from the street and returned.

Although this is a small episode in "Avatar Girl", Skinny Monkey's ever-changing and embarrassing face, and Yuan Meiyun's embarrassment when he bumped into her reading "Women's Physiology and Hygiene", are enough to make people laugh until their eyes are watery.

Suzhou People (1) 194

— By Gu Wenzong

The whistle blows repeatedly, the sound of the machine vibrates, rattling non-stop, the sound of water gradually rises and fades, and the greetings of passengers can be heard slightly. The whistle, the machine, and the sound of water gradually decrease, and the sound of people gradually increases, indicating that they are entering the cabin from outside the ship.

(The steward shouts loudly, the sound is from far to near, the sound of people breaks through the steward's shouting, and turns quiet.)

We're almost at Dagu Port! Everyone should put away your luggage! (shouting many times)

(The sound of people changes from quiet to chaotic, with the sound of suitcases, baskets, and boxes at the same time, a chaotic mess.)

(The steward knocks on the door of the official cabin, and a female guest answers from inside.) Who's knocking? - ?

Leftover Sound

The "Official Harmonica Playing Method" published by the China Harmonica Music Publishing House at No. 157, Anren Street, Xinbeimen, Shanghai, is written by Mr. Bao Mingshan, a senior member of the harmonica circle in China. The book is divided into sixteen chapters: The first chapter describes various knowledge of the harmonica, and then describes the basic musical knowledge of harmonica music. Chapters 5 to 11 detail dozens of kinds of harmonica playing methods in elementary, advanced and the latest inventions (that is, the first in the country). Chapters 12 to 14 describe the methods of breath adjustment during performance, knowledge of the stage, management and repair methods of the harmonica, etc. Chapter 15 specializes in various ensemble, ensemble, and conducting methods. Chapter 16 is an explanation of various musical forms in the world, and at the end are dozens of well-known musical pieces in long scales, short scales, and major and minor keys. The entire book is printed in fine Chinese regular script on Daolin paper, with a real price of one yuan and two jiao per copy. All major bookstores, instrument stores, harmonica groups, and schools in this city, Life Bookstore, the author's bookstore, Dagongbao, Scientific Instrument Museum, etc. are for sale both locally and abroad. It is also heard that the author of the book will personally teach various latest playing methods and play world famous songs on the Anding Radio Station (frequency 860) from now on, time Sundays from 3:00 to 4:00 PM.

"Escape from Devil's Island" Uncut 196

The "Escape from Boad Island", which is currently being shown at the Shanghai Grand Theater, depicts the inhumane facts of the "Devil's Island" prison, a French prison specially designed for imprisoning the most terrifying international criminals. The tension of the plot makes it impossible to breathe, and every scene grips the psychology of the audience, which can be called a masterpiece. The film was previously censored by the concession inspection office by one-third, which shows the seriousness of its content. It is now being shown in the theater and has not been cut by an inch. Viewers, please do not miss the opportunity. This film is indeed a masterpiece worth watching.

Cathay Showing

Sacrifice of Life 200

Movie actors who are loyal to their work often make great sacrifices, and these sacrifices sometimes even endanger their lives. In addition to actors, the sacrifices of various creatures are of course also many.

We remember that a few years ago, when "A Cut Plum Blossom" was made, a horse was beaten to death alive. Two months ago, when filming "The Lost Lamb", a dog and more than twenty birds also died. Recently, in "Go to Nature", a fawn was killed.

Horses and deer can of course be bought with money, but if it weren't for filming, they wouldn't have sacrificed their lives.
